桂省善後督署 4

組織大綱公布

（南京）國府十四日明令公布之廣西善後督辦公署暫行組織大綱如次、（第一條）國民政府爲整理廣西省一切軍事政治建設起見、在該省省政機關未經確立以前、暫設善後督辦及會辦各一員、以資治理、而専責成、（第二條）善後督辦及會辦由國民政府特派之、直隸於行政院、關於軍事事宜、受陸海空軍總司令之指揮（第三條）善後督辦於相當地點、設置公署、但會辦不得設署、（第四條）善後督辦公署、在善後期間、得按該省現在情形、關於政治、暫設民政財政敎育建設四處、每處設處長一員、關於軍事、得將全省劃爲數個警備區、每區設司令一員、均由督辦呈請國民政府或總司令部、分别任命之、（第五條）善後督辦公署之編制職掌、如另規定、（第六條）關於行政四處之組織、暫准用修正省政府組織法各廳之規定辦理、其各警備區司令部之編組、由督辦擬訂、呈請陸海空軍總司令核定、（第七條）廣西善後督辦公署辦事細則、由督辦擬訂呈核、（第八條）本大綱自公布之日施行、（十四日中央社電）

印度與猶太 36

猶太人有復國之運動印度人有自立之運動今皆在猛進之中。猶太人之謀復國。其種族雖散散處於各國之間類皆有能力以自植其勢力所少者不過無團聚之國土耳。今謀復國即欲於故土。求立足地也今據英相麥唐納之函略謂英政府對於爲猶太人所排擠而無恒業無田地之阿剌伯人。甚爲注意英政府欲及早查明何種地產可爲猶太人居留地。凡土地之取得與轉襄皆須有一種集中之管理云云猶太人領袖維斯曼遂謂。渠認今已屆與英國重行合作之時期云。是則猶太人復國之運動前途甚有希望也。

至於印度之謀自立則與猶太人異印度人原有甚之國土。所缺者政權操之他人。今因印人之自立運動遂得產生英國之圓桌會議。今聞國民大會領袖甘地已有提案。準備停止非武力反抗運動。及助成圓桌會議未了工作之條件。其條件共有四　大抵爲大赦政治犯及停止各種壓迫舉動。並調查在以前衝突時警察之行爲等。皆屬易爲之事。惟有一條。須有糾察酒店與洋布店之自由則或有問題耳然而印度日上自立之前途亦甚有希望也。

交通大學昨行工和館奠基典禮 87

中外來賓在大雪中蒞臨參加

本埠交通大學、自孫科黎照寰兩氏先後長校以來、對於校舍建築、亟謀擴充、曾定有五年與十年計畫、近兩年有執信西　與鐵木工廠之浇成、最近又開始建築工程館一所、業於去年十二月十四日動工、同月二十日、舉行破土典禮、將原有金木工廠拆卸、佈置基地、詳情業誌本報、茲聞該項拆卸工作、已告竣事、因於昨日、舉行該館奠基典禮、先期由該校校長黎照寰氏、電請鐵道部長孫科來滬、并柬邀滬上中外聞人參加、是日瑞雪紛飛、天氣甚冷、而參加者仍極踴躍、來賓中計有日本代理公使重光葵、法國副領事韓士禮、上海電力公司總工程師E·I·Ed　at、槇昌洋行代表何錦恩、美國鋼鐵公司代表鮑其斯、瑞士蘇爾壽公司代表麥士德·等數十人、於上午十時三十分舉行典禮、開會如儀後、首由黎氏報告、繼由孫科氏訓話、禮畢、即冒雪羣赴館址奠基、並攝影始散、茲將黎孫兩氏演詞、分誌於後、

黎校長報告　部長、來賓諸君、今天是我們交通大學舉行工程館奠基典禮、因爲今天下雪、不便到外面去行禮所以臨時借用這個敎室來舉行、并請部長指示、中外來賓指敎我們很感激而且非常榮幸、現在的交通大學已有三十五年的歷史、過去經過幾番改革、才成功了目前的情狀、但是近十年來、學校　各種建設都陷於停頓、原因是財政困難、直到前一年、孫部長擔任本校校長將交通大學整個的建設、預定了五年和十年的計　、一方面從精神上提起交大的精神、一方面從物質上來從新建設、依此計劃於是新宿舍（執信西　）便於去年竣工、第二步建築了本工廠第三步便是工程館、去年十二月十四日動工、二十日舉行破土典禮、計價二十四萬一千九百兩電料等裝置還不在内、合計需洋五十萬元、原來預定今年八月可以完成、因爲今年下雪比往年厲害的　故工程不能依預算規定或者要九月初帮能完工、趁這個機會、我們學校　在十月或十二月、舉行三十五週年紀念慶祝典禮、工程館也同時舉行開幕禮长準備舉行一次工業展覽會、希望各位來賓於時到校指敎各同事各同學共來籌劃這一個重大的慶祝典禮現在請孫部長訓話、

孫部長致詞　各位來賓敎職員、學生在過去兩年當中、本席在本校曾說過交通大學是中國國内的専門學校、是有光榮的成績和悠久的歷史的、在過去一十五年之中、由本校造就的國内建設人才很多無論在政府機關裏·或社會上都可看見、由這種歷史上的光榮、當然使我們　得满足、不過學校之造就人才是不能離開國家需要和社會精神、國家需要增加、我們大學便也要日　發展方能達到交通大學　創立而維持到現在的用意現在、中國已經進入和平建設的時期、以後國家需要當然非常之多、同時工商業的振興也極感到人才的需要、如此、國家社會所需要的専門人才、旣然增加那末本校造　専門人才的力量、也要同樣增加起來、本部本校因有鑒於此於是决定了一個讦劃來促使本校的發展、首先便是來從事物質上的建設兩年來已經有相當的成績這次工程館之建設實際本校在幾年以前就定了這個计劃、凌校長的　候也曾發起不過當時因爲財政困難、政府没有辦法、因之便不能實行建造直到現在才有完成的希望今天是奠基典禮、我們希望本年内全部建築落成、在落成後不僅是交通大學增加了設備、可以說是在全中國敎育界、國立大學中闢·新·元、工程館之建造、於本校發　上有莫大的關係我希望無論是敎職員或者學生都要從此更精益求精的去开究學問、研究實用的科學、今日研究了、明日就可爲社會服務、要把各種實業振興起來、共同努力去發揚光大不　是本校的光榮、也就是國家社會的幸福、這就是本度參加典禮所貢獻的意見、

各業稅則會續陳營業稅意見 92

續呈財部文

本市各業同業公會稅則研究委員會、昨續呈財政部云、南京國民政府財政部鈞鑒、案奉鈞賦字第一一九四五號批内開、呈一件、呈爲推派代表請願糾正浙省營業稅條例、並隨時考核指正、以符大綱、祈鑒核以卹商艱而利商業出、呈悉、查浙江省營業稅條例草案、業經該省府咨送到部、本部正在逐項審核、其營業分類及稅標準徵收稅率等項、如有超越部訂大綱及補充辦法之規定者、應候分别修正後、咨復該省府、轉飭財政廳、遵照辦理、仰即知照、此批等因、奉此、具見鈞部關懷民瘼、下風逖聽、無任感　、惟查江浙兩省所訂營業稅率、多有起越訂部大綱及補充辦法規定之處、謹爲鈞部約略陳之、幸埀察焉、（一）查各省營業稅綱要、除奢侈營業及其他含有應行取締者外、至多不得超過千分之二、而江浙兩省府所訂稅率、大部分超得千分之二以上、顯與綱要規定相牴觸、且土貨洋貨各别徵稅、尤與補充辦法第七條相違反、此應請鈞部予以嚴格糾正者一也、（二）查營業稅應就營業徵稅、而江浙兩省府所訂稅率、均以物品爲單位、實蹈百貨釐金捐之覆轍、啓胥吏骚擾之門、且與營業稅之命名、更相　反、此應請鈞部嚴格糾正者二也、（三）查營業稅之徵收、應以有賣買行爲者爲限、而市上所謂莊客者、並無搆成賣買之行爲、例如滬上蛋廠、設莊内地、祗買不賣、又如紗布業、海門南通一帶設號收布、另立莊於滬上、不過爲承轉裝運之便、如果此等莊客、亦須繳納營業稅、不啻一種賣買行爲、而繳納兩重營業稅、此在江浙兩省府所訂營業稅率内、並無明文規定、將來徵收時、自多糾紛、此應請鈞部轉予列入、將此等莊客、一律免繳營業稅者三也、以上理由、完全根據各業所陳而集成、務請鈞部體念商艱、對於修正江浙兩省營業稅時、凡政府别有規定在千分之二下外、一律不得超過千分之一、整賣部分、照四分之一徵稅、以符大綱規定、其徵收辦法、應仿照安徽省政府所訂、依照營業額比例辦理、庶杜騷擾、至並無賣買行爲之莊客、應免徵營業稅、以免重疊、臨電惶悚、不勝待命之至、

前夜至昨午降雪十二小時

馬路上積雪計達一尺有餘

入春以來、雨雪連綿、昨日之雪尤甚、蓋自前夕起、突由濛濛細雨、變爲雪珠、晚間六時後、每降一陣、輙停片刻、降時珠粒頗大、着瓦有沙沙之聲、不獨途行受苦、抑且擾人清夢、迨交午夜、又由珠而雪、瓣瓣梅花、團團柳絮、隨風飄舞、直至昨午方停、歷十二時之久、屋脊積雪咫尺、柔枝枯木、胥被壓倒、各街道更如粉舖玉砌、頓成一銀色的上海、因大雪而所得之見聞有足紀者、率錄之如、次

忙煞清道夫　各處積雪旣多、清道夫乍積、有數處之交通、清晨時變爲阻斷、繁盛之區、雖各項車輛、不稍停止、然雪經車轍之輾、則化爲潦、行人苦之、

黃包車居奇　黃包車夫乃乘機居奇、較平日增値倍蓗、適逢廢歷年關商界大結束之際、收帳人員、値此雨雪載途、更有行不得也哥哥之嘆、

電車難開行　本埠連日天氣甚寒、前日盡日大雨、並時落冰塊、屋瓦剥啄之聲、儼同暑天降雹、前晚竟夕大雪、直至昨日中午方霽、馬路積雪、達一尺左右、早晨華租兩界電車一律停駛、截至中午方始陸續開出、午後一時三十分許、公共租界靜安寺路於南京路一帶所裝電線、因受大雪關係、一時缺乏電流、竟使往來該處之一二三五六七等路電車、均即停頓、不能開駛前進、在沿途休息、約有二十餘分鐘、俟電流充足後、始行恢復交通、

電話受影響　閘北電話局中興路太原坊東首一叚話線、被積雪壓斷者、有二十餘根、均埀在馬路間、形似亂頭髮、行人不知者皆遠避、恐被觸電、滬閔南柘路陸河涇及斜土路間一帶、本無人烟、地方遼闊、電話局所立之電桿、在十日晚大雪時已吹斷不少、尙未及修理、而十三晚又是大雪、故電桿已多數遭厄、電綫均墮在地上、通話困難、又吳淞寳山等電話、昨日全部不通、淞陽電話公司昨發各用戶通告云、敬啓者、連日大雪、致路綫全部損壞、修理一時無從着手、不得已暫時停止通話、謹此通知、

米菜來源少　大雪不止、米船被阻、來滬稀少、據米店中之市價、每石又漲起數角、同時菜販裏足來滬、小菜價目、亦增起數倍、貧民無不呌苦、

茶棧經理被控侵佔 125

計達三萬元之鉅

北山西路一零八號源昌新茶棧、係屬合資營業、股本洋一萬元、分爲十股、經理紹興人王久成、亦股東之一、近忽被其他股東聯名控告侵占欵項三萬餘金、昨由特區地方法院葛推事開庭審理、原告各股東、公推李琢卿到庭陳述、李係女性、惟佔股份較多、據李訴稱、源昌新創自十八年廢歷十月間、被告王久成、僅半股、計五百元、彼任經理至今、侵占欵項、竟達三萬元之巨、惟其舞弊手段甚高、初猶無從查獲其破綻、嗣經詳核、始發現有數筆賬目、不相符合、如被告成記戶收入二千九百餘元、而總清簿則無此欵、諸如此類、不下數起、又所付之保險費一項、查

圖禁烟當局準備公賣之傳聞、紛至　來、各方人士奔走相告、函電紛馳事非原因、　據鑿鑿海關　客　、已承當局之委託、道行公賣章程之起草、聲稱辦理烟稅能手之　基鴻又以財部之命令、率領關務署　　耀　從周之楨　前往台　調查當地鴉片公賣辦法圖爲彷效之張本、當地華僑異常震駭、紛電本會嚴重搞爭、同時接近禁烟當局之伍連德、又公然在報上主張實行鴉片公賣、並將該文刋行單行本、分送國内外、伍連德身任本會委員、乃發爲此等言論、不但違反本會整個之主張、亦違反其個人素來之主張、士各有志、未能强同言論自由、無可厚非然本會應鄭重聲明、對伍氏個人之言論、絕對不表同情也、最近赴台調查公賣之李基鴻、與公然主張公賣之伍連德、均經正式任命爲禁烟委員會委員、而二月十三日時事新報所登該會委員長劉瑞恒、向日日社記者之談話、亦未明白否認公賣、是則禁烟當局採取公賣之政策、已在着着進行準備中遠非絕無根據者可知、本會同人、素秉總理之遺訓、人民之付託、從事拒毒之運動、期促烟禁之實施對於鴉片公賣之政策、本多年之研究、作各國之考察、以經騐及調查之所得深知其百弊而無一利、爰經常會通過表示堅决反對、本人無畏之精神、作反公賣之抗爭、茲將管見所及分條陳述如下、貢諸國人、（一）鴉片公賣乃政治道德之總破產鴉片爲亡國滅種之毒物、公賣乃列强施於殖民地之侵略政策、故其對本國人絕對不許吸食犯者處以十年監禁惟對我國僑民則放任之、其處心積慮、可以慨見、今苟行諸本國、則何殊自殺取殺人之毒品、以法律而准許人民吸食、爲籌餉之方法、誠萬古所未見、中外所未聞、萬一實行、足以釀成我國政治道德之總破產、爲全國人民所共棄、稍有良心之人、苟無以縱毒籌餉爲可行者、此鴉片公賣之一不可也、（二）鴉片公賣乃違背國際信義、自英人以鴉片輪入我國後、朝野人士、痛心烟禍、極力抗爭禁烟先進唐紹儀首先發起、訂定中英禁烟條約、是後各國又簽訂海牙禁烟條約均經我國簽字、嚴厲禁絕國内鴉片、是後屢次國際大會我國代表均根據政府及人民公意、提出反對列强在殖民地、施行鴉片公賣政策、竭力攻擊要求取消、最近外交部於一月九日、發表禁烟宣言、亦明白抗議、列强於鴉片公賣國際禁烟會議、我國代表吳凱聲目遵照該宣言、在大會提出抗爭統查我國前後對外之言動對於公賣始終反對、今如取而自行、則國際地位、喪失無餘國家信用、從茲破壞思念及此不寒而慄、此鴉片公賣之　不可也（三）鴉片公賣、乃違背總理遺訓查總理生平、對於鴉片深恨痛絕、曾於民國十三年發表拒毒主張明白聲明鴉片營業、絕對不能與人民所賦予權力之國民政府兩立、又云、苟有主張法律允許烟土之營業、海關放任鴉片人口、以充裕餉源、即爲一時權宜之計、均爲民意之公敵苟負責之政府機關、爲自身之私便、對鴉片下旗息戰、不問久暫均屬賣國之行爲、等語總理手造民國、其遺敎爲萬世所遵從萬不可違背苟有主張鴉片公賣者、實違背其拒毒之遺訓、此鴉片公賣之三不可也、（四）鴉片公賣乃破壞黨綱與法律國民黨綱、明白規定、禁絕鴉片之流　國民政府之法令、對鴉片之流　、亦主張完全禁絕再三再四、歷經明令公佈、民國于七年十一月間中央舉行全國禁烟會議、通過完全禁絕鴉片之議案四十四件當國要人議會演講、亦一致主張完全禁絕不藉鴉片爲稅源、到會諸代表上自國府各院部長、下逮各國代表均向總理宣　禁絕鴉片事實俱在中外咸知今苟放棄禁絕之政策、而實行公賣將置國民黨綱·禁烟法律·與第一次全國禁烟會議於何地、禁烟法律非等兒戯、可以朝發　改出爾反爾此鴉片公賣之四不可也（五）鴉片公賣將使烟禁每况愈下、提倡鴉片公賣者、每痛詆現行禁烟法律之失敗、殊不知現行禁律之無法實行、非禁律之罪實官廳奉行不力之罪也、當局對於現行禁律、未見雷厲風聲、對於歷次大員運土案、吸烟案、軍人種烟庇運案、雖證據確鑿、均未見依法懲辦、以致今

日軍人運土、成爲公開之秘密、高居獎職者、常爲破壞禁律之罪人甚以破壞禁律爲體面、以經營土業爲財源於人民守法、何殊緣木求魚、兩湖鴉片特稅公然自毁禁律尙欲責現行禁律之無法實施、誠屬不解故今日當務之急、在尊重現行之禁律發揮其精神、以實力促其施行、先辦違法之大員、以風全國之民衆、若棄禁律於不顧、而採用公賣政策、則人民將更失望、烟禁將每况愈下此鴉片公賣之五不可也、（六）鴉片公賣、乃促政治之退化、查鴉片流毒雖深、而满清末年、當局鑒人民之疾苦、識國際之大勢、尙能與英人訂十年禁絕之約、雷厲風行、苟有違法者、不分上下、一律懲辦、以達禁絕、爲舉世所稱道、民國初年、烟禁嚴明、徐世昌任總統時、且不惜三千五百萬金、購買英人存土、付之一炬、以示决心、今以革命之政府又値内亂平定、訓政聞始之時、乃有公賣鴉片之主張是直承满清所能爲者北洋政府所能爲者、我國民政府竟束手無策、吾人深倡前此鴉片旣經一度禁絕、今日之政府、苟下决心、亦未嘗不能禁絕苟不奮發毅力、而反採取公賣籌餉之計劃、不管自促政治之退化、此鴉片公賣之六不可也、（七）鴉片公賣將重蹈　化之覆轍、鴉片公賣、在我國已屢次實行、而均歸失敗、最近之例、如民國十六十七年間財政部在江浙施行鴉片公賣、醜態畢露、弊　百出、名爲政府籌餉而實際則政府收入、不及預算四分之一、而鴉片之銷售、則十倍於私　之時代、其中黑幕可想而知、當時因人民　反對國民政府派參事曾伯興　來滬調查、其提出中央之報告、痛言公賣烟土流弊滋多國府鑒於此法之不可行因下令取消、今苟欲實行鴉片公賣、不　重蹈已　　化之覆轍、結果終致得不償失此鴉片公賣之七不可也（八）鴉片公賣、務使政權更形混亂、今主張鴉片公賣、常痛言各省軍人私收烟稅、不下萬萬兩、　人私義、於國庫無浦同如將中飽之欵歸諸國庫、殊不知今日中央禁烟、各省軍人間尙有所顧忌一且公賣、將使軍人吏有所藉口、無不明目張膽、大徵明稅、飽其私義、　不致因中央公賣、而盡繳烟稅於政府、苟一旦中央有能力使之將烟稅盡繳政府、保不如以此能力而使之禁烟、古人云、上下交征利而國危矣、故今日若實行公賣、必使各省軍人大開財源、鞏固其位置結果更使　局混亂、而不可收拾、此鴉片公賣之八不可也（九）鴉片公賣必至取消無期、鴉片公賣爲籌餉之富源、各國殖民地、均恃爲政費最大宗之收入、故十年來、雖經我國屢次抗議均無法取消、良以收入旣鉅、一旦放棄、勢所未能、財部前在漢口、設兩瀀持稅處雖名爲暫時、今則一再延期、不肯取消、因利厚而放棄不忍也、我國之設　金、亦屬一時權宜之計、至今始得取消、可見始作　者、流害之無窮也、鴉片公賣、或主十年或主十五年、每年可收萬萬元以上將來欲其於　限期間取消、萬無其事、主張政府公賣何殊引猛虎而嘗人血、必至欲罷不能、此鴉片公賣之九不可也、（十）鴉片公賣必致增烟民、鴉片公賣旣以籌餉爲其目的之一、辦理之人無一不極力擴充其銷路、以豐收入、結果必至烟民日增烟禍日烈、南洋英荷各屬之前車、可爲殷鑒、海峽殖民地、及馬來半島、華僑烟民、佔全體百分之二十以上、我國烟禁廢弛、無可諱言、然吸烟人數、以比例計之、僅及英屬四分之一、此等情形、可爲明戒、此鴉片公賣之十不可也、總之鴉片公賣、有百弊而無一利國家經濟困難、應求根本解决之道、萬不可飤　止渴致遺無窮之禍、謹以所見佈諸宣言、所望國人羣起響應、國家幸甚、民族幸甚、

伍連德談話　國聞社去伍連德傅士、前以私人資格發表禁烟意見、供國人共同研究與考慮致引起各方之特殊注意、記者以禁烟問題、爲全國所屬目、而伍傅士德　久　其所發言論自亦爲讀者所願聞昨特　訪伍博士於九江咱號辦公處茲錄其談話如下、余（伍自稱、前所發表「流毒已極之鴉片問題」一文純爲個人目睹中國數十年來、「鴉片流毒、已達　點、今日遍及於全球、故鴉片間題、　非單純與局部之問題、實爲全世界亟應共同注意之麻醉品間題、不　以中國受害爲最烈耳、余爲中國人、一生研究醫藥、除爲謀世界人類之幸福外、愛國之心固未嘗一日去懹也、故回國服務、幾二十年、言行舉措、當亦爲國人所深悉、至本人對於鴉片一物、深悲痛絕、認爲人類之莫大毒害、尤爲吾中華民族之奇　巨敵、乃自海牙簽約以還迄已二十年日言禁烟、而烟氛增盛侈言拒毒、而毒漫全國、國外之嗎啡廠、更復加工趕製輪華麻醉品之數量、亦頻增記錄、但聞國民拒毒聲浪、而未見有根本拒毒之辦法、即治標辦法如予烟民以戒烟機會之戒烟醫院至今亦未見設立連德　屬國人目擊心傷、爰集數十年之經騐、參酌中外情形、悉心考慮不揣議陋而發表一文並非陳貢於當局、亦非代表任何機關團體之主張、更非喪心病狂之徒而含有不可告人之私隱、乃四　民衆共應研究之問題中之個人的一種意見耳目的在期望將烟毒澈底禁絕、使我中華民族能有發揚光大之一日、深願國人將毒害無窮之鴉片問題毋再僅　直線上觀察而加以深切的研究、則千慮中或有一得堪供大家討論也尤望新聞界予以精審之鑒别列論推敲、以供烟政當局之參考、而醒國人之烟夢云

中國合作學社鑒於合作事業之發展、端賴實際經營之得人而實務人才之培養、遂爲急不容緩之事、緩有合作社職員訓練班之舉辦、經執委會推請章鼎峙　勉成唐啟宇等負責籌備以來、業已將次就緒、經决定本期招收學生四十名、内二十名須經考試及格、另二十名則由各有關係機關保送、凡具初中畢業程度、年齡在十八至二十五歲之間者、均得報名投考、凡經考取學生、除膳費自理外、各費均免、宿舍亦由該社供給、訓練期限、爲六個月、敎課爲經濟槪論、合作槪論、消費合作經營論、信用合作經營論合作薄記、商算、珠算、商業常識、合作法規等九門、並有特别演講及實習等門、訓練班扯設在南京紅紙廊、定於三月一日開課、即日起凡有志投考者、可向上海博物院路北京路口該社事務所、或南京紅紙廊中央政治學校消費合作社任何一處報名均可、考試日期、爲二月二十六日、屆時在上海南京兩地同時舉行云、

金融標金醞釀狀態 150

掉期多方貼出七兩外、昨二月十四日標金狀况、複亂靡常、適逢掉期、故提前半小時、於晨八點三十分開市、而三月掉四月期、茲由多頭貼出、睚早初預做七兩餘至八兩、正式開市照掛牌七兩三錢、旋後七兩半前後、午刻計七兩、尙有一部份未曾掉完、而三月份條子照例槪無交易、大都改做四月期、惟開盤以爲七百七十四兩七錢、午時收盤七十四兩一錢、較上日略遜九錢、此乃照四月期掛牌爲標準、

四月期上場市呈蘊伏　昨四月份已上場矣市價初产後堅、復後時見蘊狀、前市共有十兩、之差度、同業心理離異莫定、若元茂永泰康潤丙興等皆有買進、恒興元亨大連帶等大致賣出也、殆匯票似趨鬆動、掛價未動、海外銀市續已狂跌、但不以爲動、緣歐市買方汪怠、於是金價尙平、嗣因買者活潑、遂見漲象、復以廣帮等脫手、目滙票轉優爲絀、乃市氣已處萎軟之境、破進八十兩以内、午時稍呈穩堅、厥後計爲八十一兩光景、此週間市况之變幻頗烈最高低價竟有五十四五兩廻顧、統核尙漲七兩八錢、昨逢週六、午後停市云、自早間四月份開盤七百八十二兩、繼出宏利物品等買進、漲爲八十七兩五錢、至大條銀又低落十六分之五、銀價狂跌一分半私電亦小去一分六二五、然美國初稍售出、旋後賣者缺少、故人心則平、旣而志豐永售出、當即降至三兩半、俄而元茂永恒興元等上場購買、兼因華比買六月美金二十八元、正金吸三月英金一一九三七五、故金價一哄而高、九點零達八十八兩此後大德成福餘萬興順利來售、遂即貶落七兩餘、先令開出時爲八十兩○五錢、掛牌勿更、内部平平、僅隔五六分鐘、漲至八十二兩五錢、恒興生大元亨等相繼脫手、急轉下風、計跌五兩、十點零猝爲七十七兩五錢、惟匯票站住、至後丙興震昌祥及套頭等均進、故逐步高翔、計猛漲七兩餘、直至十點一刻計達八十五兩一錢、恒餘恒興續售、十一點半退爲八十兩○五錢、旋後交易鮮少、而價略加一兩餘、計八十二兩二錢、迨午刻收盤爲八十一兩一錢、重已抑至八十兩有零、查半日最大價八十八兩、最小價七十七兩半、計有十兩○五錢差次、物品早開八十三兩五、午收八十兩○五錢、揭價仍爲八百六十四兩六錢、計撳八十四兩以後八十六七兩、午時八十四兩、豋賬二月七十一兩、三月七十四兩、四月八十一兩、補水七十一兩、

一得之言霜紅

老年之樂。含飴弄孫。靑年之樂。蜜月旅行。

聽幼稚生唱歌。如學語　鶑。聲聲悅耳。觀小女郎跳舞。如穿花　蜨。翩翩欲僊。

向吝嗇富人借錢。怕看他一副尷尬面孔。與伶俐婦人講話。難猜他一條彎曲肚腸。

舉債者。貧窮之大本營。好勝者。失敗之先鋒隊。

名山名水。好月好花。是上天賜人行樂之恩物。求利求名。言情言愛。是世人自尋煩惱之歧途。

婦女盛妝。不特鷹財。有時且足誨盜。子弟讀書。縱不上達。亦可免入下流。　　你要便宜。人亦要便宜。得便宜即失便宜。生不放手。死總要放手。好放手時且放手。

不如意事常八九。全在自己寬懷。可與人言無二三。何必向人訴苦。

陳友仁佚事 162

程·志·政·

前國民政府外交部長陳友仁氏。近自海外歸來。其行動至爲國人所屬目。客有談其佚事者。因摭記之。

陳氏之蜚聲全國。其功績實在於漢口英租界之收回。時與陳折衝樽爼者。爲英國之參贊阿瑪利氏。議定後。即待雙方簽字。詎翌日陳與阿瑪利會見時。突拒絕簽字。蓋英國軍艦數艘開泊江干。陳氏認爲不满也。阿旋令軍艦撤退。議始成。當時各國無不聞訊色變。譽之爲鐵腕外交家。而百餘年來弱國無外交之中國。竟得揚眉吐氣。國人之同情於陳氏。從可知矣。

當寗案發生後。各國公使。會商對付我國。於是以公使團名義提出抗議。時陳猶在位。得抗議書後曰。彼整個而謀我。我當分化之。於是分别答復。其措詞亦輕重不同。果也奏效如神。各國均紛紛單獨與我國謀妥協。不幸陳以時局變化而去位。事遂中擱。惜哉。

陳產於南洋羣島。自幼即在海外。故雖精邃英法文。而獨不諳華語。亦一缺憾也。

首都興造花園住宅區紀略 163

綠·珠·

金陵自古名城。有龍蟠虎踞之稱。國民政府奠爲首都後。僡形矞皇典麗。凡百建設。亦已次第進行。最近更有興造花園住宅區之擬議。是則羅馬巴黎不得専美於前矣。茲將首都興造花園住宅區之緣起計劃等項。分述於次。

緣起　南京市當局以爲市内人口日有加增。住宅缺乏。現有樓宇。多在城南一帶。而自下關訖於鼓樓間。逶迤十餘里。居戶寥落。頗形荒凉。自應力求開發。以資繁盛。又爲整理市制。改良住宅。及繁榮下關至鼓樓等處之市面起見。迺有興造花園住宅區之必要。

計劃　就大方巷古林寺一帶。分區興造花園住宅。每一區之面積。約自四百畝至五百畝之間。求其有林泉之勝。而城中之喧擾。區内土地。除公用者外。均准私人繳價承領。並得依照規定樣式。興造新式住宅。如是。首都之蔚然大觀備矣。

步驟　現在首先着手第一區之興造。計占地六百畝。位於三牌樓中山路之西。鼓樓之北。地點旣稱適中。地勢亦復高峻。一經開闢馬路。與中山路幹綫相銜接。行駛公共汽車。交通自屬便利。第一區完成後。再繼續推廣。使將來衡宇相望。如入藝術之塲。其最大之目的。固不僅解紓居住困難已也。

佈置　每區之興造。除照規定樣式外。並建公共園亭。愉資行樂。辦理公共學校。以重敎育。其它如運動塲游戲場中央大會堂等等。無不力求完備。其最重大之工程設備。即按戶裝設自來水。現在着手之第一區。尤注意於公共園亭之建設。務使區内林木繁殖。田園花竹彌望皆是。居斯地者。大有城市山林之槪。將來推廣至第二三區。則依山築路。住宅就山腰建築。風景尤爲幽蒨。不啻爲瑞士之縮影云

畫苑新談 164

蒼·蒼·

自六合展覽及蜜蜂社消寒會次兩展覽後。海上愛美者。頗屬自葉渭莘氏作品。渭辛所作。山水花草。流利融渾。無寒乞相。無鄙倍思。洵爲清才。蓋氏旣秉先德指發先生之敎。又與一亭堇叔諸老輩游。宜其一日千里。兩次會中所陳。如大幅山水。愚曾爲一詩張之。又柳燕白貓諸幀。皆各極雋遠渾茫之致。扇面諸屏。尤經百練。自非凡響。平居論畫。氏嘗側重靑藤。而不以白陽爲然。故其畫矯健處。乃類靑藤。然白陽託興之淡遠。用筆之簡斂。宜爲畫人所不廢。則絢爛之後。歸於平淡。渭　方年少。自不必斤斤學此而久後必知白陽之長。可斷言也。海上畫家。傖俗無論矣。其有矯絕塵者。每有清而不雄。超而不沈。直而不曲。枯而不潤之失。渭辛雄矣潤矣。能於揮灑時。力求沈著頓挫之致。則其造詣。何可限量。吾爲此文。又不特僅爲吾黨張目已也。。還質渭辛。或不河漢斯言。（未蓋章）

紀薩菩薩人鎭龍岩 165

霆·

薩菩藶者。閩之閩侯人。即大名鼎鼎之薩鎭冰上將也。樂善好施。大有大慈大悲救苦救難觀世。音菩薩之宏懷。故世以菩薩號焉。去年三省會勦共匪。菩薩曾携帶數萬金。隨軍到龍岩放賑。岩民戚同父母。頌聲戴道。一六事變。勦共部隊回師計盧。菩薩移居適中永福。指導防共工作。此次勦共軍再克復岩城。菩薩於一月二十二日由永福來岩。岩民及黨政軍人員出郭歡迎者數萬人。途爲之塞。爆竹聲與歡呼聲震天。菩薩身衣粗布長褂。雖年逾耳順。而精神頗　鑠。下簥步行。向歡迎者一一點首。由歡迎代表導入招待所要息。城内外满貼歡迎標語。如「歡迎菩薩心腸的薩上將鎭冰。」「歡迎大慈大悲救苦救難的薩上將鼎銘」「歡迎救民於水火的薩菩薩。」「薩菩藶是被難民衆的救星。」「薩菩薩萬歲」等等。五光十色。極一時之盛云。（未蓋章）

醬麯 166

秋·郎·

開門七件。無非飤食。烹飪百味。端賴油鹽。而醬油一品。亦爲此中之要索。烹魚炙膾。幾有一日不可無此君之槪。唯年來百物昂貴。醬油之次者。一入饌中。不覺其鹹。反覺其酸。有所謂「太油」或「醬油精。」味固鮮美。然除家庭中用以調羹外。若廛中包飯作等。殊罕用之。以其售價高昂也。茲有友人言。日本新發明醬麯一種。其色黝而微黃。每粒如遊戲品中之骰子大小。價頗低廉。置十餘粒於大紅花菜碗中。加以鹽粒。取沸水冲之使满。以筯攪之。立即融化。略無渣滓。取瓢嘗試。味實不在太油下也。並聞杭人某君。以此種調味新品。當爲國人所樂用。且亦有利可圖。將集資開設公司。向日本購大批原料。一方與杭地鹽商訂立合同。作大規模之製造。運銷全國云。

聽書小誌 167

平·水·

說書一道。出自姑蘇。娱樂之一也。海上日來各書場。競相舉行會書。不侫暇時輒往一聽。名擋說書。逐日輪流。頗饒興趣。爰就各擋名家略一評之。　　沈儉安薛筱卿雙擋珠塔。頗受歡迎。沈之彈唱雖微有沙音。而善於用腔。說白表情。恰到好處。薛則善於彈唱。字音清晣耐聽。堪稱珠連璧合。

楊乃武一書。說者甚少。李伯康以此得名。說時中齒清楚。唱調有勁。爲其獨到處。雖非完全吳音。（渠係潤裕社）然亦頗動聽。

黃兆麟之三國。久著聲名。緣其說時聚精會神。一起呼應。開打姿勢。表演尤佳。其書可說一載。洵不易也。

趙筱卿父子之描金鳳。堪稱拿手好書。（小卿父鶴卿即以此書享名）小卿年齒雖老。說白唱調。仍一絲不苟。而起相入神。尤屬難得。餘若魏鈺卿之唱調多韻。趙稼秋之喉音清脆。許繼祥之說白老練。均屬上駟人才。海上繁閙震人。能於暇時一聆說書。亦消遣之一法也。（不受酬）

蝦餅魚圓之製法 168

醉·痴·生·

臘尾年頭之肴核。厥味以「蝦餅魚圓爲最雋。故家庭多備之。然製之不得其法。或太老。或太嫩。味即遜色。余家所製。則頗爲合法。而物美價廉。尤非市售者所可企及。茲述其製法如下。藉備居家者之嘗試焉。

蝦餅。先以生猪油入小石臼中搗爛。（石臼新者有石屑。不可用。）乃以小蝦去壳。取蝦仁入臼中同搗。再加入鷄蛋數枚。（連黃打碎。）又鹽及陳酒少許。（如蝦一斤。用猪油一兩。鷄蛋二枚。鹽一小匙。多則類推。（打匀後。置入手中。揉成圓式。旋做旋投入冷水鍋中。俟做好後。再入火煑沸。即取起。連湯收貯。如天冷。可藏多日不壞。如須炸食。做時即入油鍋中。煑至淺黃色取起。蘸焦鹽或辣醬油食。或再用冬菰冬笋黃芽菜等同煑食。

魚圓。以靑魚（白魚亦可。）去皮骨。用刀背搗爛。再以刀口吹細。加入熟猪油。鷄蛋靑。（先打透。）菱粉。（水調。）鹽及陳酒少許。）如大靑魚一尾。帮蛋靑六七枚。餘酌用。）同杵至細膩爲度。揉成圓形。旋做旋投入冷水鍋中。再煑沸取起。連湯收貯。

短訊　蘇州五卅路公園。睚上年十二月舉行金魚會公開展覽後。即從事添缸購種工作。比聞金魚種類之收集最多者。首推該園。其預定計劃。擬於本年孵卵後。另闢水泥池塘十個。並於該園北部新　之數畝廣之池塘中。悉數養魚。一俟小魚長成。開始發售。所得收入。俾資開支云。又聞該園職員吳君。獨自在廓外鄕村。覓得一地。専事飼養細種。即利用種種科學方法。使其發育健全。作將來提倡魚業之先導。所業雖小道。必有可觀者。至於吳下一般藝魚家。近已成立一會。互研心得。並從事編訂金魚學専書發行。現方在編輯中云。（紫徵）

出版界消息　梅花館主主編之正氣三日刋。已出至七十九期。内容豐富。印刷精良。現爲優待定戶起見。凡自二月十五日以後之新定戶。槪贈梅花館主手書之四尺楹聯一副。（五尺亦可通融）外埠定報。全年計大洋二元二角。該報館址。在上海雲南路育仁里一五六號云。

水仙清話 169

沈·瘦·若·

水仙雅號金盞玉盤。種有二。曰單葉。曰千葉。千葉較貴。人都珍之。翠葉素　。清香雅潔。其風韻之足稱者。昔人詠之屢矣。丁此嚴寒天氣。冰檻雪窗間。清供一盆。對之不禁悠然神往。余因於靜觀中察得此花之特點有四。誌之以供清話焉。　　水仙之性。宛如幽嫺貞靜之女子。默默寡言。不自驕矜。而自見高潔。其品致比之息夫人實無多讓。若論其色。則雪貌冰姿。亦冷豔。亦潔艷。凌波仙子。與夫縞袂仙人。堪與其匹。香則清徵澹遠。不厭多聞。可與蘭作友。以視玫金粟。俗膩多矣。其味之最足耐人尋者。在淡而不薄。雅而不幽。如飤遠年醇酒。如對元人畫幅也。

南洋游記 170

九月一號。印度友人ＮＡＧＡＨＷＡＬＴＥ邀食印度飯。厥名拿戈瓦弟。意爲龍也。又證道會秘書拿戈拿通亦龍之意。萬慧師語我。君於印度已得二龍矣尙不知耶。余問印人多以龍名乎。如昔者龍樹。萬曰。大抵以龍名者。當爲好奇之人。平常人亦少以名也。拿戈瓦弟爲一美術家。作畫吟詩。獨身十年矣。長英文。而素食。二龍及印學生索食者多。據醫博士周光贊久於印者。言印人旅館飯店素食者遍地皆是。世界上人性善者算印人也。是日與拿戈氏先飲印度咖啡。其味甜於中國式。余不慣飲之。印人杯多用黃銅。其飲法殊可異。彼非如我惟杯就唇而飲者。乃一定如鳥之仰其項。而以杯中茶水自然灌於口中。此一定之習慣。拿戈語我。印人飲水杯。决不與唇接。乃仰而灌入故也。余常見印人飲。殊未注意。今如其敎。乃時時察之。拿戈之言不誣也。旣入飯店。純素無葷物。其食法用方塊蕉葉。舖於桌上。乃置飯菜於上。有玉蜀黍及辣菜葱。蓋忌葷而尙辛辣品。不用　而爲我特設勺义。如西餐所用。印人當然以手進食。依如法顯侢所言。有一事應注意。印人各食。各人不可以器觸他人食物。爲大不敬。不獨食物爲然。凡用具器物如烟袋茶杯布等。切不可輕以手觸之。有時一人買物。未買妥而以手觸之。遂致賠償云。但以我所見。在緬甸之印商。尙未有此俗也。余食其飯。因其蕉葉上亦頗有香味。二人一餐。凡十四安拿。未满一元。不算貴。然比中餐亦不賤也。中餐在此地者如我日在美珍飯店所食。每餐三安拿。茶甚佳矣。余近亦不敢勸人素食。因出門素食。甚不便也。印度人生活簡單。思想高尙。故甘地之復古派學術。乃能大放光明。據人云。甘地之苦行無抵抗。亦惟印人能從之。若他國民則不能也。由來人文生於地文。余以此言爲然。將來至印度。須察其地理所生之文化也。

1931.02.15

Legislative Yuan Passes Company Law Enforcement Act 1

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 131st meeting on the morning of the 14th at 8:00 AM. Thirty-six members were present, including Niu Yongjian and Jiao Yitang. The meeting was presided over by President Hu Hanmin, with Secretary-General Li Wenfan. The agenda items were: (1) Review and amendment of the draft law on the organization of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission. Resolved: referred to the Legislative Affairs Committee for review. (2) Report of the Commercial Law Drafting Committee of this Yuan on the drafting of the Company Law Enforcement Act. Resolved: amended and passed. (3) Report of the Legislative Affairs Committee of this Yuan on the review and amendment of the provisions for permanent vice ministers in the organization laws of the various ministries of the Executive Yuan, uniformly changed to executive vice ministers. Resolved: passed. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 14th)

Xu Yuanquan Arrives in Shashi 2

Remnants of Bandits in the Meitian Lake Area Eliminated

(Hankou) Xu Yuanquan arrived in Shashi early on the 14th and has already issued orders to the Sichuan, Hunan, and Hubei armies to jointly suppress the He bandits in two routes. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

(Hankou) The Rong and Xu brigades are assigned to oversee the clearing of the countryside in Mianyang. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

(Hankou) It is said that a bandit suppression conference will be held after Fan Shisheng arrives. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

(Hankou) The Zhang Brigade of the 48th Division has eliminated the remnants of bandits in the Meitian Lake area and is proceeding to Gong'an to suppress bandits. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

(Hankou) Xia Douyin returned to Hankou from Huangzhou on the 13th. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

(Hankou) He Chengjun still plans to inspect western Hubei. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Hankou) Li Mingzhong will immediately go to eastern Hubei for inspection. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Hankou) Xu Langxi, Chief Staff Officer of the Third Army Corps, went to Beijing on the 13th. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Hankou) The Third Army Corps Headquarters issued an order on the 13th to each division and brigade to recommend personnel who contributed to the suppression of the rebellion for rewards, four from each division and two from each independent brigade. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

Fourth Route Army Stationed in Hunan to Suppress Bandits 3

He Jian Welcomes Xiao's Division into Hunan

(Hankou) Miao Meiting, liaison officer of the Fourth Route Army stationed in the Third Army Corps, was summoned back to Hunan by He Jian on the 13th. According to him, Chiang ordered the Fourth Route Army to station two divisions each in western Hunan, southern Hunan, and Pingliu to suppress bandits. The remaining units will support Changyue. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Hankou) The 11th Division of Luo Zhuoying, under Chiang's order, is being transferred to Jiangxi and will depart from Yueyang immediately. Their defense will be taken over by the Tong Kun Brigade of the Fourth Route Army. The Chen Cheng Division will be responsible for protecting the northern section of the Hunan-Hubei road. (The 13th)

(Hankou) He Jian telegraphed Hankou on the 13th, welcoming Xiao Zhichu to enter Hunan to assist in suppressing the remaining bandits in western Hunan. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Hankou) He Jian telegraphed Tu Jin'yu, inviting him to enter Hunan. It is said that Wang Ding will go to Nanchang first in the next few days. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

Guangxi Rehabilitation Supervisory Office 4

Organizational Outline Announced

(Nanjing) The National Government promulgated the Provisional Organizational Outline of the Guangxi Rehabilitation Supervisory Office on the 14th, as follows: (Article 1) The National Government, for the purpose of reorganizing all military, political, and construction affairs in Guangxi Province, will temporarily establish one Rehabilitation Supervisor and one Co-Supervisor before the provincial administrative organs are established, in order to govern and be solely responsible. (Article 2) The Rehabilitation Supervisor and Co-Supervisor will be specially appointed by the National Government and will be directly subordinate to the Executive Yuan. Regarding military matters, they will be under the command of the Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force. (Article 3) The Rehabilitation Supervisor will set up an office in an appropriate location, but the Co-Supervisor may not set up an office. (Article 4) During the rehabilitation period, the Rehabilitation Supervisory Office may, according to the current situation of the province, temporarily establish four divisions for political affairs, finance, education, and construction, each with a director. Regarding military affairs, the entire province may be divided into several garrison districts, each with a commander. All appointments will be made by the Supervisor upon request to the National Government or the General Headquarters, respectively. (Article 5) The staffing and responsibilities of the Rehabilitation Supervisory Office will be stipulated separately. (Article 6) The organization of the four administrative divisions shall temporarily follow the regulations of the various departments of the revised Provincial Government Organization Law. The organization of the various garrison headquarters shall be drafted by the Supervisor and submitted to the Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force for approval. (Article 7) The detailed rules for the Guangxi Rehabilitation Supervisory Office shall be drafted by the Supervisor and submitted for approval. (Article 8) This outline shall come into effect from the date of its promulgation. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 14th)

Jin Army Commanders Confer on Disbandment Matters 5

Disbandment Method Completely Resolved

(Taiyuan) Commanders Shang, Xu, Yang, and Fu held a meeting at headquarters on the afternoon of the 12th to discuss matters such as the implementation of disbandment in various units, the distribution of disbandment funds, and the defense areas. It was decided to establish road defense armies, raise 2 million for disbandment expenses, and telegraph Zhang to expedite the transportation. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

Page 4

(Taiyuan) Hu Yiling, accompanied by Song Zheyuan representing Qin Deshen, and Xu Yongchang, representing Huang Lachu, went to Shenyang on the morning of the 13th to report on the recent disbandment situation of the Jin and Song units, and to request specific measures such as disbandment pay and stationing locations. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

(Beiping) Shang Zhen will go to Shenyang within the next few days. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

(Taiyuan) The Jin situation has been completely resolved. Chiang and Zhang replied to the four army commanders Shang, Xu, Yang, and Fu in a joint telegram, saying that they were aware of the two telegrams from Qi and Geng. The brothers' overall consideration showed their hard work and they should be approved to handle the matter as proposed after appropriate accommodation. Except for informing Councilor Ji by telegram, they are asked to comply. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

(Taiyuan) The flexible measures proposed by Shang, Xu, Yang, Fu, Ji, and Geng are divided into four points: (1) Sun Chu's unit will form a road protection army, with Sun as the commander. The organization will be the same as other armies. (2) Ren Ronghong will be the garrison commander, and Zhang Huizhao will be the deputy commander. The garrison army will consist of three regiments, reorganized from Zhang's unit. (3) Li Fuying's unit will still be organized into one division, under the control of Xu. (4) Ren Zhao Chengshou as the bandit suppression commander, and the Jin-Sui cavalry will be organized into three brigades, under Zhao's command. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

Northern Financial Conference 6

Wang Tao's Remarks

(Beiping) Wang Tao said that at the Shenyang North China Financial Conference, the central government's designated taxes will be gradually implemented after the 13th. The principles for offsetting the losses from the abolition of likin taxes in various provinces have been decided and will not increase the burden on the people. Efforts will be made to save money first, and the municipal administration expenses of Beiping will also be reduced as appropriate. As for education expenses, Zhang has discussed a permanent solution with the central government. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

Sino-Japanese Telegraph Negotiations 7

(Nanjing) The Sino-Japanese telegraph negotiations continued on the 14th. The draft contract for the Shanghai-Nagasaki line was largely agreed upon. Negotiations will continue on the 16th, and the agreement may be signed before the 20th. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

Postponement of Tibet Conference 8

(Nanjing) The Tibetan conference has been postponed because the delegates are too far away and cannot arrive in May. The Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission reported the situation and received instructions from the Executive Yuan to temporarily postpone the date. The twelve goodwill delegates sent by the Dalai Lama of Tibet will report on everything in Beijing and will go south to Nanjing within the next few days. (Special dispatch on the 14th)

Current Commentary

India and the Jews 36

The Jews have a movement to restore their nation, and the Indians have a movement for self-reliance. Both are now making rapid progress. Although the Jewish people are scattered among various countries, they all have the ability to establish their own power. What they lack is a unified territory. Now, their efforts to restore their nation are aimed at establishing a foothold in their homeland. According to a letter from British Prime Minister MacDonald, the British government is paying close attention to the Arab people who are being displaced by the Jews and have no permanent occupation or land. The British government wants to determine as soon as possible what kind of land can be used as a settlement for the Jews. All land acquisition and transfer must be under a centralized management. Jewish leader Weizmann then said that he believed that the time had come for renewed cooperation with Britain. Therefore, the movement for the restoration of the Jewish nation has a very promising future.

As for India's pursuit of self-reliance, it differs from that of the Jews. The Indians originally had a vast territory, but they lacked political power, which was controlled by others. Now, because of the Indian self-reliance movement, the British Round Table Conference has been created. It is now reported that Gandhi, leader of the National Congress, has a proposal to suspend the non-violent resistance movement and to assist in the unfinished work of the Round Table Conference. There are four conditions in total, mostly for the amnesty of political prisoners and the cessation of various oppressive actions, as well as an investigation into the conduct of the police during previous conflicts, all of which are relatively easy to do. However, one condition, the freedom to inspect liquor stores and foreign cloth stores, may be problematic. Nevertheless, India's prospects for self-reliance are also very promising.

French Royalist Restoration Dream 58

Plotting to Support the Duke of Guise as Head of State

Planning an Uprising in the North After Next Year's General Election

Paris dispatch: The French Royalist Party still exists. Its members all regard the Duke of Guise, currently residing in Belgium, as the future head of state of France. Recently, the party has been very active because of next year's presidential election, and various factions are already actively preparing. According to the party's observations, the Communist Party will win an overwhelming majority in the election, causing great turmoil in the labor sector. The Royalist Party can then take the opportunity to launch an uprising, overthrow the government, and establish a monarchy. The party is secretly planning to divide Paris into several war zones, organizing 20,000 members from various locations into several teams, all under the command of a trained military officer. If anything happens, an order can be issued immediately to summon them. The party has already obtained the Duke of Guise's consent and is preparing for him to return to the country and assume the throne after its members occupy the government. Key figures of the Royalist Party have frequently traveled to Brussels recently to discuss everything with the Duke of Guise. (World)

All-India Congress Considers Gandhi's Proposal 59

Hindu-Muslim Conflict

Seventy-Nine Casualties

Reuters, Allahabad, 13th: The Executive Committee of the National Congress has begun discussing the proposal drafted by Gandhi. The proposal contains the conditions under which the National Congress is prepared to cease the non-violent resistance movement and contribute to the unfinished work of the Round Table Conference. It is reported that the conditions include (1) amnesty for political prisoners, (2) immediate cessation of all oppressive measures, (3) investigation of police conduct in various conflicts, and (4) freedom to picket liquor stores and foreign cloth stores. The National Congress is willing to declare a truce under the aforementioned conditions and then actively cooperate in the work of drafting a new constitution for India.

Reuters, Allahabad, 13th: After a Muslim who sold foreign cloth in the Benares area was killed, a major conflict erupted between Muslims and Hindus, resulting in two deaths and seventy-seven injuries. The two sides clashed in the streets, all the shops were closed, and armed military police were deployed to suppress the conflict and patrol the streets. Order has now been partially restored.

Soviet Union Adds New Jewish Administrative Region 61

British Prime Minister's Letter to Jewish Leader to Remove Misunderstandings

National News, Moscow, 13th: The Soviet authorities have newly established a Jewish administrative region in Crimea, named the Freidorf Region, which includes fifteen Jewish village soviets, two German village soviets, and eighteen mixed village soviets. Jewish farmers account for half of the population in the area, so the authorities have specially established the administrative region to show respect for ethnic minorities and to prevent the Zionist movement from emigrating.

Reuters, London, 13th: British Prime Minister MacDonald sent a letter to Weizmann, the leader of the Zionist movement, to dispel misunderstandings about the British policy on Palestine as outlined in last October's White Paper. It roughly stated that the British government is paying close attention to the landless Arabs who have been displaced by the Jews and have no permanent jobs. The British government wants to determine as soon as possible what kind of property can be used as a Jewish settlement. All land acquisition and transfer must have a centralized management until the development plan is established on a solid foundation. The British government recognizes that the Jewish Agency can absolutely prioritize the employment of Jews to manage projects funded by Jewish capital, but if unemployment becomes serious, Britain, as the trustee, will of course have to reconsider this matter. Weizmann now claims that he believes that the time has come to cooperate with Britain again and hopes that the Jews can continue to carry out economic work in Palestine.

Japanese Political and Strategic Difficulties Shift to the House of Peers 62

Anti-Government Faction Very Active

Hamaguchi Likely to Come Forward Early

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 14th: As a result of last night's cabinet meeting on countermeasures against the House of Peers, the government believes that it will be difficult to overcome the difficulties in the House of Peers unless Prime Minister Hamaguchi attends the parliament. Therefore, they all advocated that Prime Minister Hamaguchi should attend the parliament immediately. The government's view of the parliament is that no matter how the opposition parties attack with the so-called "first-stage strategy" in the House of Representatives, it can be stopped with absolute majority power. However, the anti-government faction's activities in the House of Peers are quite organized and are progressing daily. The momentum for impeaching the government on the grounds of overestimating revenue and military preparations is increasing daily. In particular, regarding the problem of Foreign Minister Shidehara's gaffe, the voices demanding that Prime Minister Hamaguchi attend the parliament are rising. Judging from the recent situation, there has been a sudden deterioration. The government seems to be implementing Prime Minister Hamaguchi’s earlier attendance in parliament, to sweep away this unpopularity, is the best policy. Therefore, it was decided that Adachi and Eki would visit the Prime Minister in the next few days to state the above matters and discuss the timing of the Prime Minister's attendance. It is reported that the Prime Minister's attendance is scheduled for around the 22nd or 23rd.

Japan Alliance News Agency, Tokyo, 14th: The House of Representatives Budget Subcommittee completed all questions on the 14th, decided to discuss it on the 15th, decided on the attitude of each subcommittee on the 16th, and submitted it to the parliament on the 17th. After passing the House of Representatives, it will be handed over to the House of Peers to hold a budget meeting for further review. The House of Peers and the government faction plan to launch a fierce attack on the government regarding important issues. The chairman of the budget committee, Lin Hakutaro, belongs to the government faction, but most of the section chiefs of each subcommittee are anti-government figures. The fate of the budget is also not very optimistic. Japan Alliance News Agency, Tokyo, 10th: Kinya questioned at the third budget subcommittee: (1) Is the drastic reduction in Japan's trade with China the result of the sharp drop in silver prices? Is there any countermeasure for this matter? (2) Does the government have any intention of convening an international conference to reform the Chinese currency? Finance Minister Inoue replied that due to India's silver disposal and China's currency reform, the accumulation of silver in Shanghai has become an unprecedented amount. Therefore, the sharp drop in silver prices cannot be prevented. As for the reform of China's currency system, it is generally expected by all countries, but currency reform is very difficult, so there is no intention to convene an international conference.

Australia's Three-Year Financial Plan 65

Reuters, Canberra, 13th: The Australian State Premiers' Conference has passed a three-year plan to deal with Australia's financial problems, including (1) a general reduction in the salaries of public employees (this item will be automatically implemented next month due to the ruling of the arbitration court), (2) a tax of three shillings and sixpence per pound on all taxable public bonds, and (3) immediate establishment of a fund to raise floating debt. The above plan will be submitted to the bank for consideration, and the State Premiers will discuss it again on February 25. It is reported that the bank may not agree to this plan.

Public Telegram

From Nanchang: For the Attention of All Newspapers. Zhang Huizan, commander of the 18th Division of the Army, led two brigades on the 20th day of the 12th month of the 19th year, in a bloody battle against the entire five armies of the communist bandits Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang at Longgang, Jiangxi, for an entire day. Because there was no support, and resources depleted, he fell into the den of the bandits. This month during winter days, sentries of the 77th Division of the National Army discovered, at the Gan River in Ji'an, a wooden box containing a human head, marked with the name of Commander Zhang. It was identified as genuine by former subordinates and relatives. Furthermore, soldiers who escaped from the bandit side reported that, after Commander Zhang's capture, the bandit leaders Zhu and Mao threatened and enticed him, but he remained steadfast and unyielding. They tortured him all day long, but the bandits were helpless. So, on the 28th of last month, they decided to cut off his tongue and kill him. The cruelty was extreme. Zhang, the late commander, studied military science in his youth and immediately showed unusual talent. He studied in Japan and Germany, always remembering his motherland, and always regarded revolution as his duty. He initially followed the late Director Tan, participating in strategy, and then engaged in the anti-Yuan campaign with General Cai E, providing much assistance. Subsequently, he served as commander and brigade commander, participating in every battle, never boasting of his merits. In the 11th year of the Republic, he resigned and went to Shanghai, uniting with comrades in the party, recruiting talents and heroes, and secretly planning. Then, he followed the late Generalissimo and Director, went to Guangdong, and held military positions. In every battle, he took the lead. In the 15th year of the Republic, he launched a major northern expedition, serving as the commander of the 4th Division of the 2nd Army, driving through the southeastern provinces, fighting hundreds of battles, shedding much blood, and being filled with excitement. In particular, in the North River and East River in Guangdong, and in Xinyu, Luzhou, Nanchang in Jiangxi, and Yisha and Guandimen in western Hubei, he was most famous for using the few to defeat the many and reverse the overall situation. Detailed accounts are recorded in the Battle Records of the Second Army in the Northern Expedition. After the National Army was reorganized, he continued to serve in his current position. Since being stationed in Jiangxi, due to frequent incidents in the Central Plains, deployments have been frequent. He only had the strength of one division to defend dozens of counties in Jiangxi. The situation was isolated and dangerous, but he never retreated. Last July, his troops went to Hunan to suppress the rebellion. The bandit troops of Zhu and Mao took the opportunity to attack Nanchang. Commander Zhang personally supervised the division's directly affiliated team, building fortifications day and night, using only a small part of the Wang brigade to defend the city. The bandit troops were forced to retreat. All of this is something that people have repeatedly praised. Commander Zhang often said that soldiers have the duty to defend the party and the country. The communist bandits have long been a problem for the party and the country. Killing one more bandit is equivalent to removing one more harm for the party and the country. Limited by circumstances, he was unable to eliminate them, but he was determined to die early. Therefore, since receiving the order to encircle and suppress them, he has been brave and went straight ahead. In this battle with the bandits at Longgang, although he knew the disparity in numbers, he vowed not to retreat. According to his usual detailed plans for suppression, none of them failed to hit the key points. However, before the plan could be implemented, he bravely went forward to his death, exhausting his strength and mind, sacrificing his life for righteousness. His remains could not be found, but his spirit returned home first. His tongue was cut off but his integrity will forever be commemorated. His death was tragic. In addition to reporting to the central government for preferential treatment to comfort his soul, we are hereby acting on the order of the Ninth Route Army Commander, establishing a funeral office in the headquarters of the 18th Division in Nanchang, and choosing a date for a public memorial service. If you are willing to send elegiac couplets and sacrificial offerings, please send them to our office in Nanchang for receipt. The Funeral Office for the Late Commander Zhang of the 18th Division of the Army.

Important News

Model Methods for Eliminating Communist Bandits in Hunan, Hubei, Guangdong, Jiangxi, and Other Provinces 67

He Yingqin Orders Strict Prevention of Female Bandits Colluding

After Requesting Instructions, Ruan Zhaochang Has Returned to His Defensive Position

Nanchang Dispatch: National Government Chairman Chiang has learned that the bandits Zhu, Mao, Peng, Huang, Fang, Shao, Kong, Li, He, and Kuang have been rampaging through the borders of Hunan, Guangdong, Jiangxi, Hubei, Fujian, Zhejiang, and Anhui, burning, killing, looting, and employing extremely cruel methods. If they are to be fundamentally eradicated, military force alone is insufficient. He has now issued a telegram to the various bandit-suppression units in the four regions, ordering them to act in accordance with the methods of treating the symptoms and the root causes, as well as exposing those in the military who collude with the communist bandits. After receiving the telegram, Jiangxi and Shandong have forwarded it to the various units in Jiangxi to be followed. At the same time, Director He, based on the report from Jiang Jianren of the Propaganda Brigade, learned that the Communist Party has dispatched many young female bandits who are going out to seduce the military. He requested that this be strictly prevented. After receiving the report, He immediately sent a telegram to the three route commanders Lu, Zhu, and Jiang, as well as to Supervisor Wang (Jinyu), ordering them to strictly prevent this. The telegrams are roughly as follows:

Telegram to Commander Lu: In accordance with Chairman Chiang’s telegram instructing the treatment of the symptoms and root causes of bandit suppression: (1) The military should strive to suppress the bandits to treat the symptoms, but it is especially important for the party, government, and military to cooperate in publicizing our party’s ideology, uniting the masses, and thoroughly clearing the villages to treat the root causes. (2) In addition to striving to suppress the communist bandits, the military should strictly abide by discipline, actively appease the masses, and absolutely prohibit disturbing the local population. (3) The military should not be satisfied with merely driving away the communist bandits or recovering cities. They should continue to pursue and suppress them until the remnants are completely annihilated. (4) Officers and soldiers are strictly prohibited from going out and carousing. The telegram also stated: It has been found that in areas such as Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Henan, Anhui, and Fujian, the communist bandit forces are actually weak, and their methods are extremely treacherous. On the one hand, they advocate communism to deceive the masses, and on the other hand, they secretly hide their names to confuse the military and the people, disrupting the local area. After that, any communist bandits who come to agitate our military, whether at the sentry line or in the military, our officers and soldiers who can expose and solve the case will be rewarded with 100 yuan. If they can arrest a communist bandit with concrete evidence on the spot, they will be rewarded with 200 yuan. Those with more serious circumstances will be rewarded separately. However, prisoners of war are not included in this rule and must not be falsely reported. I will issue another order separately. I am sending this telegram in advance, hoping that you will immediately forward it to all subordinate troops down to the lowest-ranking soldiers, so that they may all be informed.

Telegram from Director He: To Commander Lu Yong’an, Commander Zhu Yimin, Commander Jiang Jingran, Supervisor Wang Xiangting, and Division Commander Ruan Shaowen: Secretly, according to the report from Jiang Jianren of the Propaganda Brigade, and according to the confessions of female bandits who have been captured, the Communist Party has recently dispatched a large number of young and beautiful female bandits to the garrisons of our various armies to carry out seduction work, either disguised as various small vendors, or cooking and washing clothes for the soldiers, and even sacrificing their bodies to lure them. Once a relationship develops, they say that they were captured by the communist bandits and only managed to escape back. They also say that communist bandit officers and soldiers can all receive 20 yuan per month, and the treatment of prisoners is excellent. Those who surrender a rifle can get 30 to 50 yuan, and those who do not want to stay will be given travel expenses. It has been found that the communist bandits' intentions to seduce are irresistible. I hope that you will immediately forward this to your subordinates and take strict precautions. Gengchen, He Yingqin.

Ruan Zhaochang, commander of the 55th Division, and his troops are currently stationed in the Fuliang, Jingdezhen, Raozhou, and Duchang areas, with the division headquarters located in Leping. Director Ruan came to the province on the 6th to meet Director He, report on the progress of the war, the bandit situation in various defensive areas, and request instructions on the current suppression strategy. The meeting has concluded, and he returned to Leping yesterday in the snow to return to his defensive position. (13th)

Anhui Province Organizes Village Clearing and Joint Defense 68

Anqing Actively Consolidates City Defenses

Anqing Dispatch: Chen Diaoyuan, chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, due to the rampant communist bandits in various counties, causing the people to suffer beyond endurance, is organizing a Village Clearing Headquarters, with branch offices established in various counties as appropriate, in order to carry out village clearing and bandit suppression at the same time. He has submitted this proposal to the provincial government's standing committee for discussion and resolution. The organizational regulations have been handed over to the single-item regulations review committee for review and will be reported to the meeting again. Before the headquarters is established, the provincial government has approved the request from the Prepared Army Corps Headquarters to supervise and urge the various counties to expedite the clearing of the villages in order to maintain public security. It has ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to forward this to the county magistrates of the various counties, instructing them to immediately comply with the previously promulgated Village Clearing Regulations, expedite the implementation, and report back at any time. The department has also submitted the formulated joint defense measures for the various counties, which have been passed by the 161st standing committee meeting of the provincial government, and has sent these measures to the Ministry of Interior and the provincial government for filing. It has also requested that the provincial governments of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Hubei, and other provinces be notified, instructing the counties bordering Anhui Province to implement joint defense, and has issued a notice to the sixty county magistrates to comply with this and earnestly implement it at any time. Since the establishment of municipal administration in Anqing, demolition of the city walls and road construction have been actively carried out, but due to insufficient funds, the project has not been completed. Now, the municipal administration preparatory office has been ordered to be abolished, and the broken bricks and crumbling ruins in the eastern, southern, and northern gates are visible everywhere. The Prepared Army Corps Headquarters, based on a telegram from Ruan Zhaochang, commander of the 55th Division, which roughly stated that the communist bandits are rampant and the suppression of bandits in various areas has not yielded significant results, the provincial capital is the administrative hub and defense must be strict. It is said that the city walls of Anqing have been largely destroyed and should be repaired. During the suppression of the Nian bandits in the Qing Dynasty, villages and towns were all built with stockaded walls, which could effectively control the bandits, because the bandit nature of the bandits meant they could not attack cities and had no time to attack cities, so they had nothing to plunder and would disperse on their own. This is my humble opinion, and I hope you will consider it. The Army Corps Headquarters believes that what he said is not without merit, and at this time when communist bandits are rampant, consolidating city defenses is an urgent task. It has specially consulted the provincial government, instructing the Department of Construction to order the Huaining County Government to comply, strictly prohibiting the demolition and theft of bricks and earth, and ordering the Anqing Public Security Bureau to strictly prohibit anyone from demolishing or stealing bricks and earth from the city walls, and should punish them according to the law. (February 13th)

Guangdong Army Repels Li Mingrui's Band 69

The Story of Li's Band Invading Lechang

Bandit Traces Also Found in Rucheng and Renhua

Guangzhou Dispatch: After the communist bandit Li Mingrui's band escaped from Lian County into the Guangdong-Hunan border area, they encountered an ambush by the Guangdong army's Deng Regiment in the Meihua Pingengkou area, and then fled into the Lechang County area. Huang Yanzhen, the commander of the North River Bandit Suppression, immediately sent the 149th Regiment of the 63rd Division, led by Guo Runhua, to Lechang to intercept and suppress them. Later, it was learned that the band that had fled to Lechang was led by Li Mingrui himself, with more than a thousand men, while the bands of Wei Baqun and Zhang Yunyi had entered the Lan Mountain and Linwu areas on the Hunan border through Wuyang. On the 6th, a large number of communist bandits fled to Dadong and Huangdong, opposite Lechang. There were also three to four hundred bandits who fled from Huangdong to the villages near Renhua, so on the morning of the 7th, Renhua County was once again in a state of emergency. It was found that Renhua was not far from Rucheng, and Hu Liang, the communist leader of Rucheng, had gathered more than ten people, including the commander of the pseudo-detachment, Xi Zanxiang, and others, and launched an uprising in the Rucheng area on the evening of the 6th, responding to Li's bandits, burning and killing more than twenty villages. At present, bandit traces of more than five hundred people have been found in Dongtang, twenty miles from Renhua County. As for the regular troops stationed in Shaoguan, they had already urged the 125th Brigade's replenishment regiment, led by Yan Yingyu, who had returned from Guangzhou, to also rush to Shaoguan and deploy defenses in the Xingning and Renhua areas. The first battalion of the Yan Regiment had already departed from Shaoguan for Xingning on the 7th, and the second and third battalions and the directly affiliated units of the regiment continued to depart from Shaoguan on the 8th. As for the Pingshi and Lechang areas, Guo Runhua's regiment was strictly defended and suppressed. Two regiments of the Hunan army had also arrived from the Hunan border to provide assistance. Li's bandits initially planned to disturb Pingshi and were about to cross the river, but they did not expect that the Hunan army had already arrived. Li's bandits then changed their plan, most of them retreating back to the Lian County area, while local bandits Xie and Deng each went out of Lechang City to the Dacaichang area, twenty miles away. As a result, Lechang was shaken, and merchants stopped handling goods. At the same time, the Shaoping Highway cars also stopped running. It was reported that the local communists arrived at Dacaichang on the 5th, immediately sealed off the boats and crossed the river, gathering more than 3,000 people, with about 1,000 rifles. On the 6th, they advanced along the Shaoping Highway to Changduo, which is one day away from Renhua. The local communists of Xiaobeijiang rushed from Changduo to Renhua, contacting the local communists in Rucheng. Fortunately, Guo's regiment had already rushed from Lechang to Changduo to meet them head-on. They made contact with each other in Changduo, and the battle was fierce. At the same time, a battalion of Tan Langxing's regiment stationed in Renhua was also on alert against the local communists near Renhua. In the battle of Changduo, the local communists lacked bullets and were defeated by the government army, fleeing to the Hunan border. Guo's regiment continued to pursue them with the second battalion. The Guangzhou Headquarters received a telegram yesterday from Huang Yanzhen, commander of the North River Bandit Suppression, saying that Guo's regiment had searched and suppressed the remnants of the bandits near Changduo in the North River on the 6th, capturing a company of bandits, seizing forty or fifty rifles, one mortar, and several horses, and is still continuing the search and suppression. (February 10th)

Fujian Province Security Office District Bandit Suppression 70

Allocation of the Entire Province into Nine Districts

The Central Government Sends Another Team to Take Over the Defense of Zhangzhou

Fuzhou Dispatch: The Provincial Security Office has been established, and measures for bandit suppression have also been determined. The province is divided into nine districts. The first district is Chengtai and the northwest rural area, with a detachment of the Training Corps stationed in Chengtai and a second detachment stationed in the northwest rural area. The commander is Zhou Xiaopei. The second district is Gutian, Jianou, Songyang, Pingnan, and Shuikou, which are defended by the entire Second Independent Brigade of the Marine Corps and Chen Huisheng's troops. The commander is Lin Bingzhou. The third district is Fuan, Shouning, Xiapu, Zhending, and Ningde, which are defended by the First Regiment of the First Independent Brigade of the Marine Corps. The commander is Liu Gangde. The fourth district is Lianjiang, Changle, Luoyuan, and Fuqing, which are defended by the Second Regiment of the First Independent Brigade of the Marine Corps. The commander is Huang Maohe. The fifth district is Jinjiang, Huian, Nan'an, Dehua, Anxi, and Yongchun, which are defended by the entire First Mixed Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army. The commander is Chen Guohui. The sixth district is Chong'an, Pucheng, Shaowu, and Guangze, which are defended by the entire Provisional First Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army. The commander is Qian Yuguang. The seventh district is Minqing, Yongtai, and the western rural area of Fuzhou and Minqing, which are defended by all the troops under the command of the Bandit Suppression Commander. The commander is Huang Bingwu. The eighth district is Putian and Xianyou, which are defended by the entire First Battalion of the Police Force. The commander is Liang Jichuan. The ninth district is Songxi and Zhenghe, which are defended by the entire Second Battalion of the Police Force. The commander is Liu Zongyi. After the above districts were announced, Director Fang Shengtao issued a letter to the bandit suppression officers and soldiers, recounting the deep suffering of the people of this province from the bandit scourge and the need for the bandit suppression troops to maintain discipline and maintain law and order in order to relieve the people of their suffering. As for the inspection of the Provincial Defense Army, the office also plans to start with Liu Zongyi's troops first. Once completed, the original name will be cancelled and replaced with the name of the Security Team.

Zhang Zhen's 49th Division has repeatedly received telegrams from the Central Government urging it to enter Jiangxi to join in the suppression of the communist bandits, and preparations for departure have been made. However, due to the importance of the defense of Zhangzhou, a telegram has been sent to the provincial government to forward it to the Central Government, requesting that capable troops be dispatched to Zhangzhou to take over the defense. Before the Central Government's takeover troops arrive, please order Chen Guohui to dispatch two regiments to Zhangzhou to take over the defense. After receiving the telegram, the provincial government forwarded it to the Central Government, requesting that a division of troops be dispatched by sea to Zhangzhou. This has been approved, and the Ministry of Military Administration has telegraphed the provincial government, saying that it has dispatched an elite division, which will be concentrated immediately and take a ship from Shanghai to Fujian, going directly to Zhangzhou and still under the command of He Yingqin for bandit suppression. As for the unit number, it is not yet known. (February 11th)

Tianjin Public Security Bureau Arrests Communists in Large Sweep 71

Over Thirty People Arrested and Extradited for Interrogation

Tianjin Dispatch: The Tianjin Public Security Bureau received a tip from the Special Affairs Squad the day before yesterday, stating that the Communist Party of this city was holding a meeting at the Yuzhong Hotel in the French Concession on the morning of the day before yesterday, resolving to send personnel to infiltrate and work within the Jin-nan army, which is currently undergoing reorganization, with plans to depart within days. Simultaneously, the City Reorganization Committee also received this report. They immediately consulted with Zhang Xueming, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, to devise a plan for arrest. Zhang did not issue the mobilization order until 11:30 PM the night before, dispatching Secretary-General Wu Yixian to the Japanese Police Department, Section Chief Shen to the French Municipal Council, and Secretary Zhang Guanru to the British Municipal Council, to separately negotiate arrest procedures. Due to the lateness of the hour and the lack of official documents, they requested that the arrests be made first, with warrants to be issued later. After obtaining the consent of each Municipal Council, the Public Security Bureau Special Affairs Squad immediately mobilized, joining forces with the special agents of each Municipal Council to set out at 2:00 AM yesterday morning, searching the various concessions for hidden Communists. They arrested ten Communists at No. 9 Qinren Lane in the British Concession. It is reported that among them were Zeng Pilie, Li Huifang, and two women. They also arrested Du Zhensheng, Han Linfu, and others at the Yuzhong Hotel in the French Concession. Du Zhensheng previously served as Shi Yousan's representative in Tianjin and, under the guise of purchasing firearms, embezzled 250,000 yuan and fled to Dalian. Du was once engaged to the famous socialite Jin Xiuyan, and her father, brothers, and brother-in-law were implicated and remain in custody due to his embezzlement. Du came to Tianjin from Dalian this time to attend a meeting, leading to his arrest. Accompanying Du was Han Linfu, who, it is said, was a former alternate member of the Central Executive Committee who had been expelled. Unexpectedly, after convening a meeting of Communists on the morning of the day before yesterday, he was arrested in his sleep the following morning. The search in the Japanese Concession also resulted in the arrest of over ten people. Because the locations searched in the British and Japanese Concessions were Communist strongholds, a large number of Communist books and propaganda materials were seized. All personnel involved in the Communist search remained awake throughout the night. By 9:00 AM yesterday morning, over thirty people had been arrested and extradited to the Public Security Bureau by each Municipal Council. The propaganda materials and Communist books were also transported to the bureau by automobiles. Chief Zhang dispatched Secretary Zhang Guanru, Special Affairs Director Rong Ziheng, Section Chief Sun of the Third Section, and Section Chief Shen of the Fourth Section to conduct separate interrogations last night. It is reported that the Communists arrested this time are mostly important figures. Although it was not a complete sweep, the Communist Party in Tianjin has suffered a major blow.

Furthermore, the Public Security Bureau of this city previously received a telegram from the Public Security Bureau of Baoding, stating that Bai Ruizeng, the accountant of the Tianjin Huatong Automobile Company, was carrying books for the Communist Party and requesting investigation. The bureau dispatched police on the 7th of this month to apprehend Bai Ruizeng and bring him in for questioning. According to Bai Ruizeng's confession, he delivered the books with Liu Kuisheng to a school in Baoding, but he did not know the contents of the books. The Public Security Bureau will soon escort the suspect to Baoding for further action. (11th)

Henan People's Enthusiastic Protection of Mines 72

Revision of the Bo Recuperates the Fuzhong Mining Committee's Circular Telegram

Regarding the matter of the two counties of Xiuwu and Boai in Henan Province recovering the mining rights of the British Fuzhong Company, a circular telegram was issued stating: "Recently, a telegram was sent to the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, the National Government Chairman Jiang, the Minister of Railways Sun, the Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang, the Minister of Industry Kong, the Chairman of the Henan Provincial Government, and all committee members, stating: 'After the great chaos is quelled, the people yearn for governance. The most crucial task for the entire nation is to abolish unequal treaties. The contract for the Fuzhong Company's mining affairs is a most unequal treaty. Its acquisition of these mining rights lacked legitimate justification, and after acquisition, it refused to implement even minor benefits to the local people. According to the provisions of Article 41 of the contract, which deny partial or total invalidation, this contract has long lost its value. Our committee members have submitted reports to the National Government's Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ministry of Railways, Ministry of Agriculture and Mining, and the Henan Provincial Government, engaging in negotiations, but have not fully achieved our goals. As a result, the Fuzhong Company has been unable to resume operations for years. The company, aware of the difficulty in defying public sentiment, recently used the pretext of unemployed workers to petition the Central Government, requesting permission to resume operations. An investigation reveals that the company ceased operations in 1925 due to workers' dissatisfaction with their treatment, leading them to leave en masse. The public resented its breach of contract and refused to cooperate. Currently, there are no unemployed workers in Jiaozuo, nor are there any workers willing to work for the company. The company is cunningly using pretexts to deceive the government. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, failing to recognize this, has even proposed organizing a committee to reorganize the Zhongyuan Company to discuss and resolve all disputes with the Fuzhong Company. This not only ignores the truth of the past but also disregards the fervent desire of the people of Henan to protect the mines. Our committee members, for the sake of national sovereignty and the livelihood of the people, vow to never recognize the resumption of operations by the Fuzhong Company. If this is not accepted, we can only rely on the strength of hundreds of thousands of people in Xiuwu and Boai counties to resolutely refuse to cooperate and do our utmost to resist. We hereby disclose the steps to be taken: (1) Based on the various breaches of contract by the Fuzhong Company, we will proceed to cancel its contract. (2) We will do our utmost to assist in the development of the Zhongyuan Company. (3) We will assist the government in accumulating funds to repay the debt of the Daoqing Railway. (4) We will order the Fuzhong Company to compensate for losses. (5) We will resolutely refuse to cooperate with the Fuzhong Company. Loving and protecting the mines is a common desire of the people. The government and the people should be united. We earnestly hope that you will heed the public opinion, dismiss this proposal, and not only will the hundreds of thousands of people in Xiuwu and Boai be immensely grateful, but the livelihood of the 30 million people of Henan will also depend on it. The joint association of the Xiuwu and Boai committees for recovering the Fuzhong mining rights respectfully bows in winter. Our committee members, entrusted by the people of Xiuwu and Boai, are fighting to recover the mining rights. We will not cease until our goal is achieved. We still pray for the united assistance of all compatriots, party-state seniors. We urgently send this telegram, not daring to be ungrateful." The Xiuwu and Boai committees for recovering the Fuzhong mining rights bow together.

Two Small Steamers Robbed Near Wangjiangjing 73

Jiaxing Dispatch: The Ningping steamer of the Suzhou Ning Company, traveling from Jiaxing, was sailing back to Jiaxing from Suzhou on the 13th when seven or eight bandit boats were discovered in the Tang River at Wangjiangjing South Qilihui, Jiaxing County. The bandits were all armed with wooden-cased guns, pistols, and hand-cranked machine guns, ordering the steamer to stop. They then swarmed onto the steamer and tugboats, robbing passengers indiscriminately, with no one spared. In addition to luggage, everything was looted, and many passengers had their clothes stripped off. Just as the steamer was about to be robbed, the daytime steamer of the Tongyuan Company, traveling between Nanxun and Jiaxing, also with a tugboat, arrived from the direction of Pingwang and was subjected to the same robbery. When the steamer finally reached the wharf in this city, it was already late, and the passengers were mostly in a state of utter disarray. (14th)

Jiading 75

Investigating Fraudulent Donation Offenders: The Sijing River area, where the three counties of Jiaqing, Qingpu, and Shanghai meet, used to have a branch office of the Shanghai Tax Bureau. After the office was ordered to be abolished, a patrol boat was left behind, owned by Jin Bao, a former servant of the office. On the 28th of last month, three people with Zhejiang accents, surnamed Jiang and Xu, claimed to be ordered by the Jiangsu Shipping Administration Bureau to borrow the originally rented house of the office as the bureau's office, posting announcements. Jin Bao was ordered to hang a red flag on the remaining patrol boat. All passing ships had to pay a license fee of two yuan or a license fee of five jiao, and were given zinc license plates or receipts. Later, the shipowners resisted, pointing out that they were imposters. Jiang and others dared to claim, "I am Commander-in-Chief Jiang's nephew. If you resist, we will go to Zhenjiang to mobilize troops to protect us," and left under this pretext. After receiving the report, the county government ordered Song, the section chief of the County Public Security Bureau, to lead police officers from the police squad, including Gu Wen, to investigate. They found that the report was true and recovered hundreds of zinc license plates, an announcement, and a patrol boat. They returned to the county to report. The county government has ordered the police teams to investigate and arrest Jiang, Xu, and others for punishment.

Wuxi 76

The Implementation of Long-Distance Telephone Communication Between Jiangsu and Zhejiang: Li Ximou, the director of the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau, agreed to extend the scope of long-distance telephones and lengthen the lines in order to realize telephone communication between Jiangsu and Zhejiang. He has negotiated with the directors of the construction bureaus of Wuxian and Jiangyin counties to establish mutual long-distance telephone connections. Yesterday, he sent a letter to the Wuxi County Construction Bureau, requesting similar interconnections in order to achieve telephone communication.

Garrisoning Troops to Protect Railways: The first regiment of garrison troops stationed in Wuxi, led by Regiment Commander Huang Zhenwu, was ordered by the Capital Garrison Commander Gu Zhilun to be transferred to Suzhou for training. After receiving the order, Commander Huang's regiment departed for Suzhou yesterday and today in succession. The Shanghai-Changzhou section, which the regiment had protected, has been reassigned to a battalion of the fourth regiment under Commander Jiang Xiaoxian, which has been dispatched to various stations to fill the vacancy.

Robbers Rob in Xitang Township at Night: Five robbers suddenly came to the home of Lu Zhenqing, a resident of Xitang Township near Houqiao Town, Ninth District (Beishang Township), at around 1:00 AM the night before yesterday. Armed with weapons, one robber climbed over the wall and entered, opening the side door of Lu's house to let the other robbers in. They immediately tied Lu Zhenqing's hands behind his back and then entered the rooms, overturning chests and ransacking them at will. After an hour, they left with their loot. After the incident, Lu Zhenqing saw that the robbers had gone far away and checked his losses. He reported that he had been robbed of over 100 yuan in cash, as well as leather clothing and gold jewelry, totaling over 200 yuan in losses.

Request to Seal Up the New World: It was discovered on the 7th of this month that the New World Inn located under the Gongyun Bridge outside the Guangfu Gate of this county was stealing electricity. Qi, from the electric plant, discovered that the seal on the electric box was forged. After summoning both parties and a notary at the county chamber of commerce, the seal on the electric box was re-examined, revealing a suspicious point that has not yet been resolved. Now, citizens Fang Minwen, Li Ziliang, Yang Guozhen, and others have reported that the inn secretly harbors prostitutes, condones gambling, hides filth, and acts as a go-between. It not only corrupts countless young people but also harms local morals. The inn treats official prohibitions as nothing. Yesterday, they jointly submitted a report to the Department of Civil Affairs, requesting that officials be sent to secretly investigate and order the county to seal up the inn and detain the inn manager, Xie Shaojing, in order to serve as a warning.

Changzhou 77

Criminal Chen Haida Executed by Firing Squad: Chen Haida, a robber apprehended by the Wuyi County government for gathering crowds and robbing a cloth boat on the river, confessed to the charges after interrogation. The county government immediately sentenced him to death and reported it to the provincial government. The order was approved by telegram. Local News

Reiterate Prohibition of Old Calendar Customs 83

Strictly Prohibit Setting Off Firecrackers, Beating Gongs and Drums, Business Closures, and Gambling 84

Following the Gregorian calendar and abolishing the old calendar has been repeatedly ordered but not followed. As the end of the old calendar year and the beginning of the new year approach, the municipal authorities, fearing that citizens will still be outwardly compliant but inwardly resistant, have specifically reiterated the prohibition yesterday. The public notice and instruction from the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the response from the Bureau of Social Affairs are recorded as follows:

Public Notice: The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's public notice states: Regarding the implementation of the Gregorian New Year, measures were announced by the municipal government in December of last year. All activities related to the end of the old calendar year and the beginning of the new year have already been moved to the Gregorian New Year. All other bad customs should be eliminated. In particular, the setting off of firecrackers, beating of gongs and drums, business closures, and gambling should be strictly prohibited. In addition to ordering each district to diligently investigate and prohibit these activities, it is hereby urgently announced for the information of all citizens, who are expected to comply and not deliberately violate these rules, lest they be punished. This is imperative. February 14, Republic of China Year 20, Bureau Chief Chen Xizeng.

Instruction: The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's instruction states: Comply with the order. A public letter from the Bureau of Social Affairs states: It has been found that businesses and factories may not close down during the end of the old calendar year and the beginning of the new year. The Department, in conjunction with the Municipal Party Headquarters, announced and implemented these measures, and the Central Government issued a circular stating that businesses may close down for five days during the Gregorian New Year, but may not close down at all during the old calendar New Year in order to promote the Gregorian calendar and change the people's customs. The end of the old calendar year is approaching, and there is concern that there will still be business closures according to traditional customs. In particular, food and vegetable vendors are essential to the daily life of the people, and it would be inappropriate to stop their business and cause inconvenience to the people who are following the government's orders. Therefore, it is necessary to inform them in advance so as not to cause obstacles. It is appropriate to request that your bureau investigate and quickly instruct the various districts in the northern and southern parts of the city to inform the shops and vendors under their jurisdiction that they must not close down during the specified period, so as not to incur punishment. Please reply. Having received this, and having seen the file regarding the abolition of the old calendar New Year and the promotion of the Gregorian New Year, which was previously ordered to be followed by the Municipal Government's Order No. 6543, all activities related to the end of the old calendar year and the beginning of the new year have already been moved to the Gregorian calendar, and all other bad customs should be prohibited. All matters related to the setting off of firecrackers, beating of gongs and drums, and business closures and gambling should be strictly and thoroughly investigated and prohibited. Having received the foregoing, and in addition to the public notice and reply, this order is issued to the chief, who is expected to comply and strictly enforce it. This is imperative. January 14, Republic of China Year 20, Bureau Chief Chen Xizeng.

Response: It has long been proclaimed and forbidden, in conjunction with the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs, that businesses, companies, and factories may not take holidays under the pretext of the end of the old calendar year and the beginning of the new year. The British American Tobacco Company in this city reported that its workers in the Pudong factory had requested leave for the old calendar New Year. In order to follow the Gregorian calendar, the factory did not allow leave. Now that the end of the old calendar year is approaching, most of the workers have left the factory without permission, so they are requesting instructions from the bureau in order to handle the matter. Yesterday, a response was received stating: It is found that during the end of the old calendar year and the beginning of the new year, from February 15th to 24th of the Gregorian calendar, no holidays may be taken under any pretext. If any businesses, companies, or factories take holidays without permission, they shall be ordered to pay their workers double wages for each day. If any workers take leave for reasons other than weddings, funerals, or illness, their wages will be deducted twofold. If the leave exceeds ten days and affects operations, they may be dismissed. This has been announced to the public by this Bureau in conjunction with the Municipal Party Headquarters in Public Notice No. 5096.
