Record of the Nantong College Board of Directors Meeting 136

Report on the Registration Process and Resolution to Plan Funding

Organize Base Property Reclamation and Request Government Subsidies

Chu Minyi, Chairman of the Nantong School Board of Directors, and He Yushu, Vice Chairman, convened the second Board of Directors meeting in Shanghai on the tenth of this month. The details are listed below:

Attendees: Chu Minyi, Rong Zongjing, Qian Xinzhi, He Yushu, Zhou Zhongqi, Zhang Xiaoruo, Wu Jizhi, Xu Gengqi, Yu Youren (represented by Zhang Xiaoruo), Li Shizeng (represented by Chu Minyi), Zhang Yiou (represented by Li Yongzhen); Observers: Zhang Xiaoruo (President), Li Yongzhen (Department Head), Zhang Wenqian, Zhao Shizhen, Zhang Junwu (Head of Base Property), and others.

Report Items: Chairman Chu reported (1) After the organization of the Board of Directors was established and approved by the Ministry, an application was submitted for school registration. The Ministry of Education sent personnel to inspect the school and deemed it qualified. However, it was required to have three colleges for enrollment. The school originally had three departments: agriculture, medicine, and textiles. The textile department could not be considered a college, so the Ministry temporarily approved the registration under the name Nantong College. When three colleges are established, the old name Nantong University can be restored. (2) The school has an affiliated middle school, which was previously included in the application submitted at the same time as the university. Now, according to the regulations for registering private schools, it is necessary to request the Department of Education to approve the registration. A separate form has been prepared by the Board of Directors and submitted for approval. (3) According to the regulations of the Board of Directors, in addition to permanent directors, the term of office is six years, with one-third being re-elected every two years. A re-election should be requested. (4) Due to the busy schedules of the directors, it was difficult to convene the Board of Directors, so the meeting was delayed until today. Many matters need to be discussed regarding improving school affairs, developing base property, planning funding, and reviewing and approving final accounts. President Zhang is now invited to report.

President's Report: (1) The school's academic atmosphere is good, teachers guide well, students are disciplined, and teachers and students treat each other with sincerity, with very little estrangement. The school rules are well observed. In the future, efforts will be made to rectify them at any time to prevent the spread of bad habits. (2) The three departments are all practical subjects, emphasizing practice. Those who fail monthly, term, or graduation exams must take supplementary exams or repeat the course. Academic performance is combined with practical research performance to determine the score, along with conduct grades. This is notified to the family at the end of each semester, so students can study earnestly. (3) According to a survey of graduates from the three departments, few are unemployed. Their service performance is praised by all, saying they have a good habit of diligence and hard work. The graduates of the previous session all obtained work immediately after graduation. (4) The school's expenses rely on allocations from the Dasheng Yarn Factory, which are still tight. Although the school has rich base property, it is currently unable to generate income to subsidize the school's expenses. (5) The school has over 110,000 mu of base property reclamation land in the fields, which suffered significant losses due to banditry last summer. Continued rectification is still needed. A more detailed report is available.

Resolved Matters: (1) The Board of Directors shall request subsidies from the national government, following the example of Xiamen University. (2) Prepare a request to the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture and the Boxer Indemnity Fund Committee, hoping for their subsidies. (3) The President shall send personnel to inspect the various base property lands, investigate the previous performance, and, together with the Director of Reclamation Affairs, prepare a future plan for full verification. (4) The Board of Directors shall submit a document to the Ministry of Education and forward it to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, ordering the county governments in the locations of the school's base property to cooperate in protection. (5) Establish a secretariat with four secretaries to be responsible for academic, financial, and reclamation affairs, to be concurrently held by directors. (6) Resolve the method of restoring the old name for enrollment. Add a chemical engineering department to the agricultural department, or add a mechanical engineering department to the textile department, to form a college of engineering. The three department heads should first prepare a budget and submit it to the next Board of Directors meeting for discussion. (7) Resolve to recommend Mr. Cai Ziming, Shen Yanmou, and Yu Jingzhi as directors. The meeting adjourned after a group photo.

The Cooperative League of China Opens a Training Class for Cooperative Staff 137

Recruiting 20 Free Students, Examination on February 26

The Cooperative League of China, recognizing that the development of cooperative enterprises depends on obtaining capable personnel for practical operation, considers the cultivation of practical talents to be an urgent matter. To this end, it has established a training class for cooperative staff. Since the executive committee requested Zhang Dingzhi, Yu Miancheng, Tang Qiyu, and others to be responsible for the preparation, it is now ready to begin. It has been decided that 40 students will be recruited for this term. Twenty of them must pass the examination, and the other twenty will be recommended by related organizations. Anyone with a junior high school diploma, aged between 18 and 25, can apply for the examination. All students who pass the examination will be exempt from all fees except for food expenses, which they must pay for themselves. The society will also provide dormitory accommodation. The training period is six months. The courses taught are: General Economics, General Cooperatives, Management Theory of Consumer Cooperatives, Management Theory of Credit Cooperatives, Cooperative Bookkeeping, Commercial Calculation, Abacus Calculation, Commercial Knowledge, Cooperative Laws and Regulations, a total of nine subjects. There will also be special lectures and practical training. The training class is located at Hongzhilang in Nanjing and will start on March 1. From now on, those who wish to take the examination can apply to the society's office at the intersection of Shanghai Museum Road and Beijing Road, or to the Consumer Cooperative of the Central Political School at Hongzhilang in Nanjing. The examination date is February 26, and it will be held simultaneously in Shanghai and Nanjing.

Shanghai Basketball Group B, Division 3, Jianle Wins Championship 145

Defeated Qi Team 11-9 Yesterday

The final of the Shanghai Basketball League Group B, Division 3 was held at Huaxing last night. The participants were Jianle and Qi Team. Qi Team added the final touches, but finally was unlucky and only scored one point. As a result, Jianle won 11-9 and won the Group B, Division 3 championship. Gold Standard Situation Under Development 150

In addition to the seven taels posted by the swap party, the gold standard situation on February 14 was complicated and erratic. Because it was swap day, the market opened half an hour early, at 8:30 AM. The March to April swap was posted by the bulls, initially at seven taels and then at eight taels. The official opening price was seven taels and three qian, then around seven taels and a half. At noon, it was seven taels, and a portion had not yet been swapped. As usual, there were no transactions in March contracts. Most of them were converted to April contracts. However, the opening price was 774 taels and 7 qian, and the closing price at noon was 74 taels and 1 qian, which was slightly less than 9 qian from the previous day. This is based on the standard of the April contract listing price.

The April Contract Market Shows a Hidden State The April contract has already been launched. The market price was initially strong, but later showed a hidden state. The difference between the highest and lowest prices in the first session was ten taels. The psychology of the same industry was divergent and uncertain. Companies such as Yuan Mao Yong Tai Kang Run Bing Xing all bought in, while Heng Xing Yuan Heng Dalian Dai and others mostly sold out. The exchange rate seems to be easing, but the listed price has not moved. Overseas silver markets continue to plummet, but it is not considered to be moving. Because the European market buyers are sluggish, the gold price is still flat. Later, as buyers were active, there was an upward trend. Then, Guangbang and others sold out, and the exchange rate turned from superior to inferior. The market atmosphere was already weak, breaking into eighty taels. At noon, it was slightly stable, and later it was 81 taels. The weekly market situation has been quite intense, and the highest and lowest prices are as high as 54-55 taels. The total increase was still 7 taels and 8 qian. Yesterday was Saturday, and the market closed in the afternoon. Since the April contract opened at 782 taels in the morning, it rose to 87 taels and 5 qian after Hongli and others bought in. The big silver bar then fell by 16 points. The silver price plummeted by 1.5 points. The private telegram also went down by 1.625 points. However, the United States initially sold out slightly, and then there were fewer sellers, so people's hearts were calm. Then Zhifeng Yong sold out, and immediately fell to 3.5 taels. Soon, Yuan Mao, Yong Heng Xing Yuan and others came to the market to buy. At 10:00, it suddenly became 77 taels and 5 qian. However, the exchange rate stood still. Later, Bing Xing, Zhen Chang Xiang and other hedging teams all entered, so they gradually soared, soaring by 7 taels, reaching 85 taels at 10:15. Heng Yu and Heng Xing continued to sell, and fell back to 80 taels at 11:30. Later, there were few transactions, and the price increased slightly by 1 tael, totaling 82 taels. Observations on the Year-End Closings of Financial Circles 155

The silver and money industries set yesterday as the deadline to count the results of settling the 19th year of the Republic accounts by February 16. There is considerable confidence that all kinds of outstanding debts have been accounted for, and most creditors with good reputations have already settled. However, there are many who are unable to compensate for deferred payments due to unpaid or unsettled mortgages or foreign exchange. According to investigations, more than 60% of the accounts have been cleared. It is evident that the silver and money industries have been cautious in issuing loans and have used steady practices during the 19th year, resulting in favorable results. However, bad debts are inevitable, but it is still not a major concern.

One Word of Wisdom: Frost and Red

The joy of old age: playing with grandchildren. The joy of youth: honeymoon travel.

Listening to kindergarten students sing is like hearing fledgling orioles, their voices melodious and pleasing. Watching little girls dance is like seeing butterflies flitting through flowers, gracefully aspiring to be immortals.

Borrowing money from miserly rich men, one fears seeing their awkward expressions. Speaking with clever women, it is difficult to guess the twists and turns of their minds.

Debtors: the headquarters of poverty. The competitive: the vanguard of failure.

Famous mountains and rivers, beautiful moons and flowers, are blessings bestowed by heaven for people to enjoy. Seeking profit and fame, expressing love and affection, are detours taken by people to seek troubles themselves.

Women dressing up extravagantly not only seek wealth but also sometimes instruct thieves. Children reading books, even if they do not reach high positions, can also avoid falling into the lower classes. You want to be cheap, and others also want to be cheap. Gaining cheap means losing cheap. You cannot let go when you are alive, but you will always have to let go when you die. You should let go when it is time to let go.

Unsatisfactory things happen eight or nine times out of ten, all depending on one's own broad-mindedness. There are only two or three things that can be said to others, why bother to complain to others?

Anecdotes of Chen Youren 162

Cheng Zhizheng

Former Foreign Minister of the National Government, Chen Youren, recently returned from overseas. His actions are closely watched by the people. A guest discussed his anecdotes, so I noted them down.

Chen's fame throughout the country was really due to the recovery of the British concession in Hankou. At that time, the British consul, Amari, negotiated with Chen. After the agreement was reached, it was waiting for both parties to sign. Unexpectedly, when Chen met Amari the next day, he suddenly refused to sign because he felt dissatisfied that several British warships were docked in the river. Amari then ordered the warships to withdraw, and the agreement was made. At that time, all countries turned pale upon hearing the news and praised him as a tough diplomat. China, a weak country with no diplomacy for over a hundred years, was able to finally stand tall and proud. The people's sympathy for Chen is evident.

After the Nanjing Incident occurred, the foreign envoys discussed how to deal with China and submitted a protest in the name of the diplomatic corps. Chen, who was still in office at the time, said after receiving the protest, "They are plotting against me as a whole. I should divide them." Therefore, he replied separately, with different wording for each. As expected, it worked like a charm. The countries all rushed to negotiate compromises with China individually. Unfortunately, Chen lost his position due to changes in the situation, and the matter was interrupted. What a pity.

Chen was born in the South Seas Islands and had been overseas since he was young. Therefore, although he was proficient in English and French, he did not know Chinese. This was also a shortcoming.

A Brief Account of the Construction of Garden Residential Areas in the Capital 163

Lüzhu

Nanjing has been a famous city since ancient times, known as the "dragon coiling and tiger crouching." After the National Government established it as the capital, its beauty and elegance were magnificent. All kinds of construction have also been carried out in an orderly manner. Recently, there has been a proposal to construct garden residential areas, so Rome and Paris cannot claim exclusive fame for this. The origins, plans, and other aspects of the capital's construction of garden residential areas are described below.

Origins: The Nanjing Municipal Authorities believe that the city's population is increasing daily, and housing is lacking. The existing buildings are mostly located in the southern part of the city, and the area between Xiaguan and Gulou stretches for more than ten miles, with few residents, which is quite desolate. Efforts should be made to develop and prosper the area. Also, to reorganize the municipal system, improve housing, and promote the market between Xiaguan and Gulou, it is necessary to construct garden residential areas.

Plans: Garden residences will be constructed in zones around Dafang Lane and Gulin Temple. Each zone will have an area of approximately 400 to 500 mu. The aim is to have the beauty of forests and springs and to avoid the noise of the city. In addition to the land for public use, all land within the zone can be purchased by private individuals by paying the price and building new-style residences according to the prescribed style. In this way, the grandeur of the capital will be prepared.

Steps: Currently, the construction of the first zone is starting. It covers an area of 600 mu and is located west of Sanpailou Zhongshan Road and north of Gulou. The location is quite suitable, and the terrain is high. Once the roads are opened and connected to the main line of Zhongshan Road, public transportation will be convenient. After the first zone is completed, it will continue to be expanded so that houses will be visible in the distance, as if entering a field of art. The ultimate goal is not only to alleviate housing difficulties.

Layout: In addition to the prescribed styles, public pavilions will be built in each zone to provide entertainment, and public schools will be established to emphasize education. Other facilities such as sports fields, playgrounds, and central assembly halls will all be made as complete as possible. The most important project is the installation of running water for each household. The first zone currently under construction pays particular attention to the construction of public pavilions, so that trees will flourish in the zone, and gardens with flowers and bamboos will be visible everywhere. Those who live in this place will have the idea of ​​urban mountains and forests. In the future, when the second and third zones are extended, roads will be built along the mountains, and residences will be built on the mountainside. The scenery will be even more secluded, just like a miniature version of Switzerland.

New Talks on Painting 164

Cang Cang

Since the two exhibitions, the Exhibition of Six Harmonies and the Winter Gathering of the Honeybee Society, Shanghai art lovers have greatly admired the works of Mr. Ye Weixin. Weixin's landscapes, flowers, and plants are fluid and harmonious, without the appearance of coldness or meanness. He is truly a talented individual. He has received the teachings of his elders and has also traveled with masters such as Yiting and Jinshu, so it is fitting that he progresses a thousand miles a day. The items displayed in the two exhibitions, such as large landscapes, have been praised by a poem written by me. Also, the paintings of willows, swallows, and white cats are all extremely refined and full of ethereal charm. The fan paintings are particularly well-honed and have an extraordinary flavor. In ordinary discussions about painting, he often emphasizes Qing Teng and does not agree with Bai Yang. Therefore, his paintings resemble Qing Teng in their vigor. However, the tranquil indifference and simple brushstrokes of Bai Yang should not be abandoned by painters. After brilliance, one returns to simplicity. Weixin is young, so he does not need to meticulously study this, but he will surely know the merits of Bai Yang in the future. This can be said with certainty. Shanghai painters, not to mention the crude and vulgar ones, often have the faults of being clear but not majestic, transcendent but not deep, straight but not curved, and dry but not moist. Weixin is majestic and moist. If he can strive for a sense of deliberation and restraint when painting freely, then his achievements will be limitless. I wrote this article not only to promote my party, but also to ask Weixin if these words are not far-fetched. (Unstamped)

Recording How Bodhisattva-Hearted People Calm the Dragon in Longyan 165

Ting

Sa Puli is a native of Minhou, Fujian, and is the well-known General Sa Zhenbing. He is fond of good deeds and charity, and has the great compassion and mercy of Guanshiyin Bodhisattva, who saves people from suffering. Therefore, the world calls him the "Bodhisattva." Last year, the three provinces joined forces to suppress the communist bandits, and the Bodhisattva brought tens of thousands of gold coins with the army to Longyan for disaster relief. The people of Longyan treated him as if he were their parents, and their praise was endless. After the 1927 Incident, the suppression troops returned to Ji Lu, and the Bodhisattva moved to Yongfu, where he guided the anti-communist work. This time, the suppression army again recovered the city of Longyan. On January 22, the Bodhisattva came to Longyan from Yongfu. Tens of thousands of people, including the people of Longyan and party, government, and military personnel, welcomed him outside the city, causing the road to be blocked. The sound of firecrackers and cheers shook the sky. The Bodhisattva was wearing a coarse cloth gown. Although he was over sixty years old, he was still quite energetic. He got out of the sedan chair and walked, nodding to the welcomers one by one. He was led to the reception center by the welcoming representatives to rest. Inside and outside the city were plastered with welcome slogans, such as "Welcome General Sa Zhenbing, with the heart of a Bodhisattva, to calm Longyan." "Welcome General Sa Zhenbing Dingming, who is compassionate and merciful and saves people from suffering." "Welcome the Sa Bodhisattva who saves the people from fire and water." "Sa Bodhisattva is the savior of the victims." "Long live Sa Bodhisattva," etc. They were colorful and extremely grand for a time. (Unstamped)

Small Notes on Listening to Storytelling 167

Ping, Shui.

Storytelling is an art that originated in Suzhou. It is a form of entertainment. These days, various storytelling theaters in Shanghai are holding storytelling gatherings. When I have some free time, I often go to listen. The famous storytellers perform in turns each day, which is quite interesting. Therefore, I would like to briefly comment on some of the famous storytellers. The collaborative performance of "The Pearl Pagoda" by Shen Jian'an and Xue Xiaoqing is very popular. Although Shen's singing has a slightly hoarse voice, he is good at using melodies. His narration and expressions are just right. Xue is good at playing instruments and singing. His pronunciation is clear and pleasant to listen to, making them a perfect match.

"Yang Naiwu" is a book that few storytellers perform. Li Bokang gained fame for telling this story. His enunciation is clear and his singing has vigor, which is his unique quality. Although it is not pure Wu dialect (he is from the Runyu Society), it is still quite pleasant to listen to.

Huang Zhaolin's "Romance of the Three Kingdoms" has been famous for a long time because he is focused and engaged when he tells the story. His call and response and performance of fighting stances are particularly good. It is not easy to tell the story for a whole year.

Zhao Xiaoqing and his son's "Gold-Painted Phoenix" can be considered a signature story. (Xiaoqing's father, Heqing, was famous for this story). Although Xiaoqing is old, his narration and singing are still meticulous, and his engagement is especially rare. Other storytellers such as Wei Yuqing, whose singing has many tunes, Zhao Jiaqiu, whose voice is crisp, and Xu Jixiang, whose narration is experienced, are all top talents. The bustling city of Shanghai is a vibrant place, and listening to storytelling in one's spare time is also a way to relax. (No payment accepted).

How to Make Shrimp Cakes and Fish Balls 168

Zui, Chi, Sheng.

Among the delicacies at the end of the year, shrimp cakes and fish balls are the most delicious. Therefore, many families prepare them. However, if they are not made properly, they will be too old or too tender, and the taste will be inferior. The ones made in my home are quite suitable, and they are of high quality and low price, which is unmatched by those sold in the market. The method of making them is described below for those who want to try at home.

Shrimp Cakes: First, put raw lard into a small stone mortar and mash it. (A new stone mortar has stone chips, so it cannot be used.) Then, shell the small shrimp and put the shrimp meat into the mortar and mash it together. Then add a few eggs (break the yolks together), a little salt and rice wine. (For one catty of shrimp, use one tael of lard, two eggs, and one small spoon of salt. If there is more, then extrapolate.) After mixing well, put it in your hand and knead it into a round shape. Make it while you put it in a pot of cold water. After it is made, put it on the fire and boil it. Then take it out and store it with the soup. If the weather is cold, it can be stored for many days without spoiling. If you need to fry it, put it in a pot of oil while making it, and cook it until it is light yellow. Take it out and eat it with charred salt or spicy soy sauce. Or cook it with winter mushrooms, winter bamboo shoots, and yellow sprouts.

Fish Balls: Remove the skin and bones of green fish (white fish is also acceptable). Mash it with the back of a knife, then chop it finely with the edge of the knife. Add cooked lard, egg white (beat it thoroughly first), water chestnut flour (mix with water), salt, and a little rice wine. (For a large green fish, use six or seven egg whites, and use the rest as appropriate.) Pound it together until it is fine. Knead it into a round shape. Make it while you put it in a pot of cold water. Then boil it and take it out and store it with the soup.

Brief News: The Suzhou May 30th Road Park held a goldfish exhibition last December. Since then, it has been adding tanks and purchasing species. It is said that the park has the most species of goldfish. According to the plan, ten new cement ponds will be built after hatching this year. The park will also raise fish in the several acres of ponds in the northern part of the park. Once the small fish grow up, they will be sold. The income will be used to cover expenses. It is also said that Mr. Wu, an employee of the park, has found a place in the countryside outside the city to specialize in raising fine species. He uses various scientific methods to make them develop healthily, so as to be a pioneer in promoting the fish industry in the future. Although the industry is small, it must be impressive. As for the general fish farmers in Wu, they have recently established an association to exchange ideas and compile a book on goldfish science for publication. It is currently being edited. (Zi Zheng)

News from the Publishing Industry: The Zhengqi Three-Day Newspaper, edited by the owner of the Plum Blossom Pavilion, has been published to the seventy-ninth issue. The content is rich and the printing is excellent. Pure Talk on Narcissus 169

Shen, Shou, Ruo.

Narcissus is known as the golden cup and jade plate. There are two types: single-petal and double-petal. Double-petal is more expensive, and people cherish it. The green leaves and white flowers are fragrant and elegant. Its charm is worthy of praise. People in the past have often praised it. In this cold weather, a pot of narcissus is placed between the ice railing and the snowy window. Looking at it, one cannot help but feel relaxed and longing. I have observed four characteristics of this flower in quiet contemplation. I record them here for pure conversation. The character of the narcissus is like a quiet and chaste woman. She is silent, does not boast, and is self-evident in her nobility. Her character is not much different from that of Lady Xi. As for its color, it is snowy and icy. It is cold and beautiful, and it is pure and beautiful. The fairy of the water and the fairy in white are comparable to it. The fragrance is clear and distant. One does not tire of smelling it. It can be friends with orchids. Compared to roses and golden millet, it is too vulgar and greasy. The most enduring taste is in its lightness and elegance. It is like tasting aged wine, like looking at a painting by a Yuan dynasty master.

Travels in Southeast Asia 170

September 1st. My Indian friend NAGAHWALTE invited me to eat Indian food. His name is Nagowardi, which means dragon. Also, the secretary of the Testimony Association, Nagonatong, also means dragon. Master Wanhui told me, "You have already obtained two dragons in India and you don't know it?" I asked if many Indians are named after dragons. Like the dragon tree in the past. Wan said, "Generally, those who are named after dragons are curious people. Few ordinary people are named after them." Nagowardi is an artist. He paints and writes poetry. He has been single for ten years. He speaks English and is a vegetarian. There are many dragons and Indian students who ask for food. According to Dr. Zhou Guangzan, who has been in India for a long time, vegetarian hotels and restaurants are everywhere in India. Indians are considered to be the most kind-hearted people in the world. On this day, I first drank Indian coffee with Mr. Nagowardi. It tastes sweeter than the Chinese style. I am not used to drinking it. Indian cups are mostly made of brass. The way of drinking is very different. They don't drink like us, with the cup to their lips. They always raise their heads and pour the tea in the cup naturally into their mouths. This is a fixed habit. Nagowardi told me that Indians never touch the cup to their lips when drinking water. They always pour it in by raising their heads. I often see Indians drinking, but I didn't pay attention. Now, according to his teaching, I always observe it. Nagowardi's words are true. After entering the restaurant, it was purely vegetarian with no meat. The way of eating is to use square banana leaves and spread them on the table. Then put the rice and dishes on it. There are corn and spicy green onions. They avoid meat and like spicy food. They don't use chopsticks, but they specially set up spoons and forks for me, as used in Western food. Indians naturally eat with their hands, according to what Fa Xian said. One thing to note is that when Indians eat, they cannot touch other people's food with their utensils. It is considered very disrespectful. Not only food is like this. You must not lightly touch any utensils, such as pipes, teacups, and cloth, with your hands. Sometimes someone buys something, but if they touch it before it is finalized, they will have to pay compensation. But from what I have seen, Indian merchants in Myanmar do not have this custom. I ate their rice, because their banana leaves also have a fragrance. A meal for two people costs fourteen annas, which is less than one yuan. It is not expensive, but it is not cheap compared to Chinese food. Chinese food here, like what I eat at the Rizai Meizhen Restaurant every day, costs three annas per meal. The tea is very good. I don't dare to persuade people to be vegetarians lately, because it is very inconvenient to be vegetarian when going out. Indians have a simple life and noble thoughts. Therefore, Gandhi's retro school of thought can shine brightly. According to people, Gandhi's non-violent resistance can only be followed by Indians. Other nationals cannot. Culture comes from the land. I think this is true. When I go to India in the future, I must observe the culture produced by its geography.

Shanghai Market

Market News 171

The Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau announced that the silk and satin bureau at Sanmakou, Shilu, has newly arrived with a large batch of fashionable silk and satin, which have been displayed for cutting. The goods are still a new creation on the Shanghai market and are the only new products, it said.

The Sincere Company on Nanjing Road announced that the company's southern goods and tea department has smoked fish chicken legs, Suzhou and Guangdong tea snacks, candied fruits and preserves, sweet oranges and Ning oranges, lard rice cakes, which are most suitable for gifts, and will be open for business as usual today, Sunday.

The Baofang Company announced that the company's self-made Jubao Pen brand gramophone has a very wide sale. Now, in order to expand its business, it has specially set up a general distribution office at the west end of Zhengjia Muqiao in the French Concession, telephone number 12250, specializing in wholesale. And set up the first Baofang distribution office opposite the China Bookstore on Simalu Road, telephone number 12862, and set up the second Baofang Company distribution office at the east end of New World on Damalu Road, telephone number 10342, and set up the third Baofang Company distribution office at No. 265 Aiduya Road, telephone number 12250, distributing various gramophones and acting as agents for Pathé, Gaoting, Beikai, Victory, Kaiming, Great China and other records, and selling parts such as springs, diamond needles and steel needles. Its manufacturing plant is located on Xujiahui Road, the old site of the Pathé Company's woodworking factory, and the telephone number is still borrowed from the Pathé Company, it said.

The Guanshengyuan Food Department on Nanjing Road announced that, in order to facilitate retail customers, a take-out store for buns and dumplings has been specially set up in the company's retail department. Milk powder lard buns and various dumplings and cakes are very busy every day. Recently, several dozen kinds of Foshan-flavored braised and roasted dishes have been added, such as liver sausage meat trotters chicken and duck, etc., in addition to supplying customers for snacks, they are also wholesaled for sale in the take-out store, ranging from 20 cents to 40 cents each, and are stored in art paper boxes without additional charges, it said.
